#awighnamāstu#

#prathamas saṙggaḥ#
<śroñca>:1.

hana sira ratu dibya rĕṅön,
praśāsta riŋ rāt musuḥ nira praṇata,
jaya paṇḍita riŋ aji kabèḥ,
saŋ daśaratha nāma tamoli*

sira ta triwikramapita,
pinakabapa bhaṭāra wiṣṇu maŋ janma,
inaka nikaŋ bhuwana kabèḥ,
ya ta don ira nimitta niŋ janma*

guṇamānta saŋ daśaratha,
wruḥ sira riŋ wéda bhakti riŋ déwa,
taṙ malupèŋ pitrĕpūja,
māsiḥ ta sirèŋ swagotra kabèḥ*

rāgādi musuḥ maparö,
riŋ hati ya toṅgwanya tan madoḥ riŋ awak,
yékā tan hana ri sira,
prawīra wihikan sirèŋ nīti*

kadi mégha maṅhudanakĕn,
paḍa nira yaṙ wèhakĕn nikaŋ dana,
dīnāndha krĕpaṇa ya winèḥ,
ṅuni-ṅuni ḍaṅhyaŋ ḍaŋ ācāṙyya*

mwaŋ satya ta sira mojar,
riŋ anak kĕbi towi taṙ mrĕṣawāda,
ṅuni-ṅuni yan ri para jana, 
priyahita sojaṙ nirātiśaya*

saphala sira rākṣakèŋ rāt,
tuwi sira mitra hyaŋ indra bhakti tĕmĕn,
māhéśwara ta sira lanā,
Śiwabhakti ginöŋ lanā ginawé*

ikanaŋ dhanuṙddhara kabèḥ,
kapwa ya bhakti ri sira praṇata matwaŋ,
kadi mawwata yaśa lanā,
rūpa nyan agöŋ ta kīṙtti nira*

jñāna nira śuddha kadi wulan,
parāṙtha gumawé sukā niŋ bhuwana,
sākṣāt indra sira katon,
tuhun hanèŋ bhumi bhéda nira*

ikanaŋ pratāpa dumilaḥ,
suka nikanaŋ rāt yatèka ginawé nya,
kadi bahni riŋ pahoman,
dumilaḥ maṅdé suka nikaŋ rāt*

hana rājya tulya kéndran,
kakwèhan saŋ mahāṙddhika suśīla,
riŋ ayodhyā subhagèŋ rāt,
yéka kaḍatwan niraŋ nrĕpati*

hayu niŋ swaṙgga tuwi masor,
dé niŋ ayodhyāpurātiśaya,
suka nityakāla ménak,
ri rĕŋ-rĕŋ towi riŋ lahru*

sakwèḥ nikaŋ mūlya kabèḥ,
kanaka rajata lèn manik hana ṅkana,
yāṅkĕn huntu nya maputiḥ,
gumuyu-guyuŋ swaṙgga kasoṙ dé nya*

hana ta umaḥ kanaka maṇik,
kinuliliṅan ikaŋ taman rāmya,
warakanyakāmĕŋ-amĕŋ,
warāpsāri tulya rin méru*

Śpaṭika maṇik tamalaḥ-alaḥ,
satéja muṅgwīŋ umaḥ paniñjowan,
kadi pwa gaṅga saka himawān,
rūpa nya katon sutéjāśrī*

suka trĕpti saŋ naréndra,
bhuktīkaŋ bhoga tan papaḍa dibya,
niṙbhaya tan hana katakut,
sāmanta kabèḥ  masö praṇata*

saŋ kékayī sumitrā,
kośalyā ghāra saŋ naréndra tiga,
duṙggā gaṅga gorī,
paḍa nira surūpa dibyaguṇa*

sukha saŋ naréndra makurĕn,
dèwi nira kapwa yatna maniwi,
tan hana māmbĕk iṙṣya,
ri sira dèwi matūt katiga*

kadi haṙṣa saŋ mahāṙṣi,
saktèn rĕk sāma lèn yajurwéda,
maṅkana saŋ daśaratha wèḥ,
haṙṣa sira ta dé mahādèwī*

malawas sirāṙ papaṅguḥ,
masnéha lawan mahādèwī,
surasa saṅgama rinasan, 
rāgāliṅganācumbanādi nya.

mahyūn ta sira maputrām,
mānaka wèt nyaṙ warĕg riŋ wiṣaya,
malawas taṙ pānak ataḥ, 
mahyūn ta sirāgawéya yajña*

hana sira rĕṣyaśrĕṅga,
praśāsta karĕṅö widagdha riŋ śāstra,
tamoli ri yajña kabèḥ,
anuŋ makaphalāŋ anak dibya*

sira ta pinĕt naranātha,
marā ry ayodhyā purohita ṅkāna,
tātaṙ wihaŋ sira pinèt,
pininta kasihan ta sirāyajñā*

saji niŋ yajña ta humaḍaŋ,
śrī-wrĕkṣa samiddha puṣpa gandha phala,
dadhi ghrĕta krĕṣṇatila madhu,
mwaŋ kumbha kuśāgra wrĕtti wetiḥ*

lumĕkas ta sira mahoma,
prétādi piśāca rākṣasa minantran,
bhūta kabèḥ inilagakĕn,
asiŋ mamighnérikaŋ yajña*

sakalī kāraṇa ginawé,
Āwāhana lèn pratiṣṭa sānnidhya,
paraméśwara inaṅĕn-aṅĕn,
umuṅgu riŋ kuṇḍa bahnimaya*

sāmpun bhaṭāra Inĕnaḥ,
tinitisakĕn taŋ miñak sasomyamaya,
lawan ikaŋ krĕṣṇatila madhu,
śrī-wrĕkṣa samiddha rowaŋ nya*

saŋ hyaŋ kuṇḍa pinūjā,
caru makuliliṅan samatsyamāṅsadadhi,
kalawan sĕkul niwédya,
inamĕs salwiṙ nikaŋ marasa*

ri sĕḍeŋ saŋ hyaŋ dumilaḥ,
niniwédyākĕn ikaŋ niwédya kabèḥ,
oṣadhi lèn phalamūla,
mwaŋ kĕmbaŋ gandha dhūpādi*

sāmpun pwa sira pinūjā,
binojanan saŋ mahāṙṣi paripūṙṇna,
kalawan saŋ wiku sākṣī,
winūṙṣitan dinakṣinān ta sira*

Śésa mahāṙṣi mamījā,
pūṙṇnāhuti dibya patyagandharasa,
ya ta pinaṅan kinabèhan,
dé nira dèwī mahārāja*

nda tatīta kāla luṅhā,
mānak tānakbi saŋ daśarathāsiḥ,
saŋ rāmānak matuha,
i sira mahādèwī kośalyā*

saŋ kékayī sira makānak,
saŋ bharata kyāti śakti dibyaguṇa,
dèwī siraŋ sumitrā,
lakṣmaṇa Śatrughna putra nira*

ri wĕtu nikaŋ putra kabĕḥ,
pinuluŋ ḍaŋ hyaŋ lawan ḍaŋ acarya,
paripūṙṇna sira pinūjā,
binojanan dé mahārāja*

matuhānak naranātha,
winara-waraḥ maṅajya wédāstra,
bhagawān wasiṣṭha maṅajar,
nipuṇa wruḥ sirèŋ dhanurwéda*

saŋ rāma sira winarahan,
riŋ astra dé saŋ waṣiṣṭa taṙ malawas,
kalawan antĕn ira katiga,
prajñèŋ widyā kabèḥ wihikan*

sāwara-waraḥ mahāṙṣi,
hĕnti kabèḥ tan paśéṣa kapwa tama,
karĕṅö ta sira riŋ rāt,
guṇāmānta suśīla śakti towi raray*

hana sira gadhisutaṙṣi,
yogīśwara lèn tapaswi rājāṙṣi,
wiśwāmitra ṅaran nira,
sira rumĕṅö śakti saŋ rāma*

patapan ira yā mananā,
dé nikaŋ rākṣasa krūrakaṙmma,
mahyun ta sira rinākṣā,
patapan nira dé niraŋ rāma*

naranātha saŋ daśaratha,
sira pinaran dé niraŋ mahaṙṣiwara,
gorawa saŋ prabhu pinaran,
praṇata manambaḥ sirānuṅsuŋ*

apa don iraŋ saŋ mahāṙṣi,
kita jaya riŋ mantra siddha sākahyun,
tatwa ya linolyanta lanā,
yatikā mūlya riŋ waŋ kadi kita*

sumahuṙ ta saŋ mahāṙṣi,
tan madwa wuwus naréndra yukti tĕmĕn,
kami ikihĕn wiku hana matapa,
jñāna lawan yoga mūlya juga*

ikana kunaŋ dona mami,
mamalakwa rinakṣā dé mahārāja,
hana saṅhulun mayajña,
ndan yālilaŋ rākṣasāmighné*

ikana kunaŋ yan yogyā,
saŋ rāma marā riŋ āśrāma maṅrakṣā,
śāraṇa mamin wĕnaṅa,
umatyanaŋ rākṣasāmighné*

maṅkana liŋ mahāṙṣi,
naréndra trĕṣṇa tĕmĕn ri saŋ rāma,
ndī taṙ sahuṙ tumuṅkul,
mojaṙ tā saŋ mahāṙṣi muwaḥ*

hé nātha saŋ daśaratha,
nojaṙku rĕṅönta yatna pituhun ya,
yan tan yogya kṣama ya,
jāti niŋ aswī maminta kasiḥ*

nyā dhaṙmma niŋ kadi kita,
pinakaśaraṇa dé niraŋ tapaswi kabèḥ,
salwīra niŋ katakuta,
kita tāṅrākṣā ri duḥka kabèḥ*

nyā dhaṙmma niŋ kadi kami,
mawaraha kita riŋ sinaṅguhan dhaṙmma,
puṇya lawan pāpa kunaŋ,
kami mawaraha ŋ waŋ kadi kitèŋ yukti*

brahmaṇa kṣatriyan padulur,
jāti nya parasparopasaṙppaṇa ya,
wiku tan panātha ya hilaŋ,
tan pawiku kunaŋ ratu wiśīṙṇna*

kalawan tambhāra Iké,
apan mahāśakti rakwa saŋ rāma,
yéki rānak śrī naranātha,
tatan hana paḍa nira ri kaśaktin*

ya mataŋ nya hé naréndra,
haywa ta sandéha riŋ anak jayā,
dānawa rākṣasa hilaṅa,
prabhāwa saŋ rāma hétuka nya*

nā liŋ mahāṙṣi mojar,
umenĕŋ ataḥ naréndra maṅĕn-aṅĕn,
dolayamānacitta,
képwan ta sira taṙ wĕnaŋ sumahur*

an lakwéki si rāma,
lumagé muṅsuḥ mahāṙṣi riŋ patapan,
pĕjahāwās ya kasāmbya,
apan raré tuwi tan wruḥ riŋ biṣama*

tuhu yan wruḥ ya riŋ astra,
ndā tan tahu maṅlagé musuḥ biṣama,
rakṣasa māyā ya kabèḥ,
lāwan paracidra yan papraŋ*

yapwan wihaṅe mahāṙṣi,
tak anumodā yaṙ paminta śaraṇa ṅké,
krodhā sirān salahasan,
byakta kami kabèḥ śināpa nira*

ri huwus nirān māṅĕn-aṅĕn,
sumahuṙ ta sirānumoda taṙ pamihaŋ,
om-om sājña mahāṙṣi,
yan yogyā pwa ṅhulun śaraṇā*

bālaka raray mapuṅguŋ,
tapwan papraŋ taman panon śatru,
yapwan wĕnaṅāśaraṇā,
sojaṙ mahāṙṣi tan wihaṅĕn*

dadi tuṣṭa saŋ mahāṙṣi,
madĕg ta sira māmwit muliha śīghra,
saŋ rāma sira madandan,
lumakwa marérikaŋ patapan*

saŋ lakṣmaṇa sira dibya,
sira sasuka duḥka mwaŋ saŋ rāma,
rumakĕt citta nira lanā,
dadi ta sira tumūt marĕŋ patapan*

sira magawé pratiwimba,
tuladana ikaŋ wwaŋ ulaḥ nirāṙ paniwi,
sakwan saŋ rāma tumūt,
taṙ dadi kantun asiŋ saparan*

rahina ya sakatambé māwa taŋ déśa rāmya,
lumaku ta sira kāliḥ sāmpun amwit manambaḥ,
mamawa ta sira laṅkap astra saṅhārarāja,
anakĕbi ry ayodhyā śoka monĕŋ manaḥ nya*

katĕka nira lumakwāśānti saŋ aṣṭaséni,
paḍahi haji ya ginwal maṅgalā niŋ lumampaḥ,
kumĕdut i tèṙṅĕnan māṙ bāhu saŋ rāmabhadra,
marahakĕna Alaḥ niŋ śatru tātan paśéṣa#

#dwitīyas saṙggaḥ#
<basantatilaka>:2.
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ : 14

kāwit śaratsamaya kāla nirāṙ para ṅkā,
ṅ ton taŋ pradéśa ri hawan Ira kapwa rāmya,
kwèḥ lwaḥ magöŋ katĕmu dé nira tīṙtha dibya,
udyāna lèn talaga niṙjhara kapwa mahniŋ*

tuñjuŋ putiḥ pwa ya ta-tañjuŋ abaŋ sĕḍĕŋ rūm,
kumbaŋ nya ghūṙṇnita maśabda humuŋ sadaṙppa,
lèn mandamāmruta miriṙ ya sugandha māmbö,
saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa rikaŋ kṣana tuṣṭa dé nya*

kĕmbaŋ turut sisi rikaŋ padamāṙgga lumrā,
saŋ rāmabhadra manĕhĕṙ maṅalap ta kĕmbaŋ,
mādyus sirācamana kapwa maśoca riŋ lwaḥ,
ṅkāné śilātala jenĕk ta sirān pararyan*

utphulla taŋ kumuda kapwa mĕkaṙ paḍābaŋ,
ṙyyak-ryak nikaŋ talaga yéka dumèḥ ya cāla,
byaktan katon kadi dilaḥ niŋ apuy ya molaḥ,
kumbaŋ bhramanta I ruhuṙ nya Akĕn kukus nya*

rāmya ŋ alas kadi mahā maṅilo tumuṅkul,
cāyā nya yèniṅĕt-iṅöt ya mawās rikaŋ lwaḥ,
mèdī dĕlĕg Agul-agul magĕlis ya molaḥ,
cāyālilaŋ malimunan makusut ya dé nya*

tatkāla sāmpun umĕtu pwa bhaṭāra suṙyya,
rukṣékanaŋ kumuda śūnya hilaŋ hayu nya,
sakwèḥ nikaŋ kayu kadi pwa tumūt makiṅkiŋ,
moni ŋ manuk mawurahan kaharan taṅis nya*

mwaŋ lwiṙ nikaŋ kayu kadi pwa mahā padĕlwan,
lāwan tikaŋ talaga kapwa sahaṙṣa kāliḥ,
kĕmbaŋ nya kapwa maputiḥ kaharan mata nya,
kumbaŋ umandĕl ahirĕŋ ya ta tāraka nya*

tuñjuŋ prakampita tinūb riŋ aṅin ya molaḥ,
tulyānulak kadi mahā ri laki nya mélik,
kumbaŋ marĕŋ kumuda ṅūni dumèḥ ya méwa,
iṙṣa swabhāwa nikanaŋ wini ghāra kāsiḥ*

Ṅkānèŋ alas bhramara matta maśabda mandra,
nidraŋ kidaŋ kiniduṅan juga paṅhiḍĕp nya,
caṇḍāla yékana manaḥ nya luput pwa dé nya,
Āpan pijeṙ ya rumĕṅö kalahaṅsa moni*

ahniŋ maho talaga dibya makin ya saśrī,
kātéjanaṇ sakĕna dé ni sĕnö hyaŋ aṙkka,
sindūrawaṙṇna kadi lāka mabāŋ prabha nya,
lwiṙ nyan katon kadi ta téja tĕñuḥ dadi wway*

nāhan tinoṙ ira rikaŋ wanadéśa rāmya,
n ton taŋ gagā saphala dibya pari nya wrĕddhi,
kapwākiris wahu huwus winatun ya rāmya,
saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa sahaṙśśa tumon ya saśrī*

wanwé gunuŋ-gunuŋ alĕmbu gawé nya mahwan,
yékā hawan Ira tinon ira taŋ palĕmbwan,
gopāla yékana mamöḥ rikanaŋ prabhāta,
mawwat miñak susu gawé nya maré ry ayodhya*

gopāṅgana anakĕbi saŋ makĕmit palĕmbwan,
rārā gunuŋ duga-dugā sipi maryada nya,
yaṙ ton sirāŋ humaliwat madulū rwa sānak,
wiśwāsa yan wahu mulat sapi wèḥ wulat nya*

gambīra śabda nikanaŋ mamutĕṙ ya mandra,
yāṅkĕn paḍahya nikanaŋ maṅinum magoṣṭi,
sakwèḥ nikaŋ wwaŋ amutĕṙ maṅigèl jugānton,
bāhu nya kāliḥ asiliḥ-silihan ya molaḥ*

daṙppā ŋ kidaŋ ya makidaŋ-kidaṅan ya mādrĕs,
wèt nyān śaratsamaya kāla dumèḥ ya daṙppa,
ṅkāné tĕgal-tĕgal lawan mamaṅan-maṅan ya,
saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa Alaḥ magiraŋ tumon ya*

Śuddhāputiḥ pwa ya ta mégha magöŋ akandèl,
imbaŋ nikaŋ gunuŋ i soṙ kahanan nya lumra,
dé niŋ aṅin makin agöŋ ya makin ya māwān,
lwiṙ nyān katon kadi gunuŋ himawān apūṙwwa*

lèn siṅha muṅgu rikanaŋ giripāṙśśwa moni,
śabda nya riŋ gagana mapratiśabda mādrĕs,
sakrodha maṅdèmaka liŋ nya mulat tumĕṅha,
Āḥ sihha mūḍa winaliŋ nya musuḥ nya monī*

riŋ paṙśśwa lèn talaga rāmya tinon ira ṅkā,
tuṅjuŋ putiḥ juga sĕkaṙ nya tatan hanābāŋ,
tātan katon hana ta haṅsa putiḥ maṅumbaŋ,
śabda nya mātra karĕṅö mrĕdu komalālwan*

sakwèḥ nikaŋ talaga tan hana tan patuñjuŋ,
tuñjuŋ nya tan hana kuraŋ paḍa mèsi kumbaŋ,
kumbaŋ nya kapwa muni tan hana tan paśabda,
śabda nya kaṙṇnasuka tan hana tan manojña*

tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ patapan mahāṙṣi,
sakwèḥ niraŋ wiku tapaswi kabèḥ manuṅsuŋ,
Ꜽṙ śānti puṣpa phalamūla sugandha dhūpa,
lèn wwaḥ sĕrĕḥ wway ininum panamuy mahāṙṣi*

sāmpun siromaṅan ikaŋ panamuy sutrĕpti,
māmöŋ-mamöŋ sira rikaŋ patapan mahāṙṣi,
wiśwāsa saŋ tapa kabèḥ paḍa gorawāṅliŋ,
ménak ta Uṅgwan ira riŋ patapan wisāta*

māsiḥ ta saŋ rĕṣi mawèḥ ta sirāstra diwya,
saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa parĕŋ winaraḥ maṅajya,
widyātiduṙjjaya jayā wijayā jayantī,
yékin pawèḥ ri sira dibya Amoghaśakti*

sāmpun tikaŋ aji kabèḥ tama dé nirāwās,
māmöŋ-amöŋ sira rikaŋ wanadéśa rāmya,
n-ton rākṣasī téka mamātyana donya tan lèn,
wadwa nira ŋ prabhu daśāsya si tāṭakākyā*

saŋ rāma yatna Inayat nira taŋ sudhanwa,
gaṇḍéwa dibya tumihaŋ warayaŋ malaṇḍĕp,
tĕṅgĕk nya yénaraḥ-araḥ nira tan papiṅrwan,
mūṙccān tiba maguliṅan ta si tāṭakākyā*

sāmpun pĕjaḥ pwa ya sahaṙṣa ta saŋ mahāṙṣi,
tātan hanaŋ bhaya rikaŋ patapan samrĕddhi,
māriŋ manuk muni mĕṅé matakut ya kasraŋ,
dé niŋ mahāmuni raray muni yāmicāra*

Ṅūnin hanékana si tāṭaka tāpa moni,
moŋ mona muṅgu ri guhā nya humīs awak nya,
sihhomĕhaḥ ya malapākuru yaṙ mahuṅhaŋ,
aṅhiŋ warak juga warĕg rumuruk rikaŋ rwī*

sāmpun pĕjaḥ pwa katakut nya si tāṭakākyā,
moŋ māri mabrata warĕg ya kĕnas kidaŋ kwèḥ,
siṅhātisāhasa mahas riŋ alas madasyu,
mattā ŋ liman ya pinaṅanya labuḥ brata nya*

sakwèḥ niŋ oṣadhi Anuŋ tinanĕm mahāṙṣi,
mārin nana saphala dibya parĕŋ ya mawwaḥ,
poḥ ambawaŋ wawaŋ atöb ya kabèḥ umĕṇḍuḥ,
lwiṙ nyān katon kadi sumĕmbahakĕn phala nya*

tatkāla yan rahayu ŋ āśrama pūṙṇnawrĕddhi,
saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa winūṙṣita dé mahāṙṣi,
dinyūs inaṙggha sira muṅgu rikaŋ palaṅka,
mojaṙ ta saŋ rĕṣi tumon sira dibyajāti*

hé rāma lakṣmaṇa Anāku nihan rĕṅönta,
nārāyaṇāṅsa kita wiṣṇu Awakta jāti,
sakwèḥ nikaŋ bhuwana ṅūni dhināraṇanta,
rākṣanta yajña mami dènta kamīkyayajñā*

nā liŋ mahāṙṣi sumahuṙ taŋ sira pinūjā,
sojaṙ mahāṙṣi kita tan hana saṅśayanta,
Āpan prabhāwa ni tapanta magöŋ alaṅghya,
yékān dumèḥ kami jayā ri musuḥ mahāṙṣi*

nā liŋ niraŋ nrĕpasutottama rāmabhadra,
sāmbut taŋ āyudha laras lawan astra dibya,
maṅkat sirāṅuliliṅi patapan prayatna,
saŋ lakṣmaṇéka n-aduluṙ nira kapwa saṅkĕp*

tatkāla saŋ rĕṣi kabèḥ ta winĕḥ mamūjā,
ṭandwa ŋ musuḥ tĕka parĕŋ sumahab ya rodra,
ṅkānèŋ laṅit kadi ta mégha sĕḍĕŋ gumantuŋ,
danṣṭrokarāla ya sihuŋ nya kilat paḍa nya*

saŋ lakṣmaṇékana wawaŋ Umulat tumĕṅha,
wĕṇṭaŋ laras nira sudhīra maṅékapāda,
tātan salaḥ r-araḥ-araḥ ya riŋ aṙddhacandra,
śiṙṇnāpasaḥ mati kabèḥ nya taman paśéṣa*

teṇḍas nya ghoratara rāhu paḍa nya rodra,
śabda nya bhīṣaṇa rikaŋ gagaṇan paṅohan,
lāwan Awak nya maṅawandha tibā gumĕntĕr,
sakwèḥ niraŋ tapa kabèḥ matakut tumon ya*

mārīca yékana tuha nya masö masĕṅhit,
māyā yatéka pinasaŋ nya masö tumandaŋ,
saŋ rāma taṙ wighani śūra sudhīra maṅsö,
mojaṙ siraŋ nrĕpatiputra mahā marīkṣā*

mārīca mūḍa Apa donmu riŋ āśrama ṅké,
kon māṅsabakṣaṇa ri saŋ wiku taṙ pamāṅsa,
yapwan Ĕmās ya kaharĕpmu ri saŋ tapaswī,
tan drĕbya saŋ wiku ṅaranya Atītaduḥka*

Ꜽ rāmabhadra Atimūḍa dahat mapuṅguŋ,
tātan Ĕmās pinakadon mami yan para ṅké,
taṙ māṅsa tan Apa mahāṅrabhasā juga ṅké,
dhaṙmma swabhāwa mami rākṣasa śatru niŋ rāt*

mighnèŋ ayajña Umattī wiku tan padosa,
nā dhaṙmma niŋ asura-rākṣasajanma jāti,
mūṙkkātisāhasa mamañcana bañcanĕŋ rāt,
krūra swabhāwa mami tan hana sādhubuddhi*

nyaŋ rāt kabèḥ ya rabhasāṅkwa taman paśéṣa,
wèhĕnku taŋ bhuwana dadya Alas ya śūnya,
Āpan swabhāwa mami rākṣasa sāhasèŋ rāt,
nā liŋ nya śīghra sumahuṙ nrĕpaputra rāma*

yan rākṣasaprakrĕti duṣṭa ya tūtanamwa,
jātinku śuddha karatun ya ta tūtanaṅkwa,
ṣakwĕḥ nikāŋ adhama rākṣasa śatru niŋ rāt,
tātan pataṅgwa sahana nya ya patyanaṅkwa*

mārīca ko kalana mūḍa taman panoliḥ,
atyanta sāhasa rikèŋ patapan mahāṙṣi,
ko tan pasāra trĕṇatulya ḍukut mahumpaŋ,
méraŋ aku g-lawana ko laku mūṙ saka ṅké*

nā liŋ nirāṙ adĕgakĕn ta laras nirāgöŋ,
bāyabya yéka pamanaḥ nira bāyu madrĕs,
mārīca rākṣasa kapuk juga tan pasāra,
kontal katūb ya tamatan papuliḥ muliḥ ya*

sāmpun katūb kapalupuy pwa ya dé niŋ astra,
indrādi déwata sahaṙṣa manādhukāra,
Ꜽ rāma hé daśarathātmaja sādhu dibya,
nā liŋ nirāṅhudanakĕn sira puṣpawaṙṣa*

ménak manaḥ nira mahāmuni yan payajña,
niṙwighna tan hana kuraŋ rikanaŋ pamūjā,
lāwan ta yajña nira niṙmmala niṙwikāra,
sāmpun mahoma Umuwaḥ ta mahāṙṣi mojar*

Ꜽ rāmabhadra kita dibya Anugrahanta,
bhūlokapāla kita liṅkwiki yan hana ṅké,
sāswaṙgga dé nikana taŋ prĕthiwī hiḍĕpku,
kabwat nikan hana bhaṭāra Śacīpati ṅké*

sakwèḥ nyawakta katutuṙku tinonku maṅké,
wiṣṇwaṅśa déwata kitānaku dibya śakti,
riŋ pūṙwwakāla balirāja hilaŋ ya dènta,
kṣīrodasāgara nahan pinutĕṙtta ṅūni*

mwaŋ rāhu yékana cinakra gulū nya dènta,
kwèḥ dꜽtya dānawa Anuŋ talu dènta ṅūni,
prākkalpa dibya tĕmahanta warāharūpa,
saŋ hyaŋ lĕmaḥ kalĕbu ṅūni dhināraṇanta*

nyānuŋ rĕṅönta ratu saŋ janakojarĕṅkwa,
mahyūn sirāgawaya yajña ta rakwa maṅké,
lāwan swayambara nahan gawayĕn wanèhan,
sītā Anak nira rarā waraṅĕn malakya*

ndā tan wĕlin riŋ upabhoga lawan kaḍatwan,
trꜽlokyarājya tuwi tan ya pamĕlya rīya,
aṅhiŋ wiśésa kaharĕp nya Anuŋ siwin ya,
wwaŋ śaktimānta guṇamānta kulīṇajanma*

sītā sĕḍĕŋ nya mĕtu ṅūni laras duluṙ nya,
gaṇḍéwa dibya yatikā pinakaryari nya,
yapwan hanānuŋ umĕṭĕŋ ya mayat ya śaktya,
ya swāmya saŋ janakarājasutā tatan lén*

ndan liṅku yogya kita milwa Ataḥ marā ṅkā,
aṅhiŋ kitékana Anuŋ wĕnaṅomayat ya,
gaṇḍéwa yadyapin akas tikĕla ta dènta,
sītā Awās ya kita kéwala kahyuna nya*

nā liŋ mahāṙṣi ri siraŋ nrĕpaputra kāliḥ,
tātan wihaŋ sira parĕŋ ta masö manĕmbaḥ,
sāmpun manĕmbaḥ aduluṙ sira śīghra luṅhā,
saŋ rāma lakṣmaṇa marèŋ mitilādhirājya*

tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ pasabhān saśobha,
sök ghora ghūṙṇnita humuŋ tikanaŋ manonton,
tonton ta rūpa nira saŋ nrĕpaputra kāliḥ,
Āścaṙyya tékana manaḥ nya wijaḥ ya mojar*

hyaŋ aświno sira kunaŋ umahas mara ṅké,
hyaŋ kāmadéwa ta kunaŋ maduluṙ basanta,
Ākāra Iṅgita sulakṣaṇa rūpa sampat,
saŋ hyaŋ triwikrama kunaŋ umahā katona*

nā liŋ nikaŋ wwaŋ umulat paḍa haṙṣacitta*
saŋ rāmadéwa pinuji nya surūpa dibya,
mojaṙ ta saŋ janakarāja mulat sahaṙṣa,
saŋ rāmadéwa pinarīkṣa winèḥ ta laṅkap*

gaṇḍéwa dibya paṅalaḥ tripuréka ṅūni,
laṅkap bhaṭāra paraméśwara pūṙwwakāla,
sakwèḥ niraŋ nrĕpati ta umĕtĕŋ mayat ya,
saŋ rāma kéwala Anuŋ tumikĕlakĕn ya*

sāmpun tikĕl pwa ya sahaṙṣa ta saŋ naréndra,
tuṣṭāgiraŋ hati niraŋ janakādhirāja,
dé niŋ prabhāwa nira saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,
mojaṙ ta saŋ janaka riŋ bhaṭamantrimukya*

saŋ rāma yogya rasikā ta siwīn i sītā,
sampat kulīna tuwi yowana śaktimānta,
undaŋ ta saŋ daśarathāt laku śīghra méṅgal,
saŋ rāmadéwa waraṅĕn ya ta pājaranta*

nā liŋ niraŋ janakarāja rikaŋ kinonkon,
luṅhā ḍatĕŋ tumama mājaṙ-ajaṙ ya wrĕtta,
kagyat siraŋ daśarathān winaraḥ Inundaŋ,
tātaṙ wihaŋ sira pinèt teka śīghra méṅgal*

tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ mitilādhirājya,
maṅkat sagorawa siraŋ janakāṙ panuṅsuŋ,
nānā prakāra panamuy paribhoga yogya,
mojaṙ ta saŋ janakarāja mulat sahaṙṣa*

hé nātha saŋ nrĕpati śūra mahāprabhāwa,
dhaṙmmāṙtha kāma gawayĕn tuwi dé naréndra,
mitra hyaŋ indra kita déwata tulya sākṣāt,
bhāgyan tĕmĕn kami ḍatĕŋ naranātha maṅké*

rānak naréndra guṇamānta suśīla śakti,
saŋ rāmadéwa tamatan papaḍérikaŋ rāt,
sītā ya bhaktya ri y-anak naranātha tan lèn,
nāhan prayojana naréndra pinèt marā ṅké*

nā liŋ niromĕtu ta saŋ wara rājakanyā,
pahyas huwus hana kabèḥ masĕkaṙ sugandha,
maṅsö manĕmbaḥ i siraŋ naranātha kāliḥ,
lāwan siraŋ nrĕpatipūtra surāmabhadra*

sāmpun manĕmbaḥ aduluṙ sira kāṙwwa muṅgaḥ,
ṅkānèŋ umaḥ pawaraṅan paḍa haṙṣacitta,
méraŋ-iraŋ hana giraŋ nira yan pasaṇḍiŋ,
tan yogya yan wuwusa wèḥ paturū nira ṅkā*

luṅhā ŋ kulĕm rahinakāla wijil hyaŋ aṙkka,
mamwit ta saŋ daśarathomulihéry ayodhyā,
lāwan Anak nira ta rāghawa lakṣmaṇāmtaḥ,
sītā tumūt saparicāra parĕŋ umaṅkat*

lāwan Amātya bhaṭamantri kabèḥ manuṅgaŋ,
luṅhā sirāta liwat iŋ wanadéśa rāmya,
kāwit hana pwa maṅawit wiku rodrarūpa,
pañjaŋ nyawak nira satal mamikul ta laṅkap*

wok bris kumis nira piśaṅga jaṭā nirāwyaŋ,
saŋ rāmabhaṙggawa ṅaran Ira tan hanoli,
saṅkèp sĕnaddha Umasö ta mapatrayuddha,
mojaṙ nirādara wuwus nira tan hana twaŋ*

Ꜽ rāmadéwa Aku rāma ṅaranku riŋ rāt,
yan śakti ko papagakĕn n-aku yan prawīra,
ko mātya dèṅku Athawā Aku mātya dému,
wĕṇṭaŋ larasku yadiyan tuhu śaktimānta*

nā liŋ niraŋ paraśurāma mapatrayuddha,
sītā gĕlāna kumĕtĕṙ ta manon apūṙwwa,
mojaṙ ta saŋ daśaratāsi manĕmba-nĕmbaḥ,
saṅka ry asiḥ nira maputra lawan mamantu*

hé jāmadagni kita śakti gahan rikèŋ rāt,
kwèḥ śaktimānta ratu śīṙṇna pĕjaḥ ya dènta,
mahyun ta mapraṅa puwiḥ kalawan si rāma,
tan yogya dènta ya raray tuwi hīnaśakti*

nā liŋ narādhipa maminta kasiḥ manantwa,
tan pārĕṅö paraśurāma sirābhimāna,
saṅkā ri daṙppa nira tan panahā-nahā wwaŋ,
tā śakti liŋ nira wanèḥ sira kéwalātaḥ*

laṅkap nirātiśaya dibya magöŋ apañjaŋ,
mwaŋ hrū pawèḥ ri sira saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,
yapwan wĕnaŋ mayat i ko Alahāku dému,
bhaktyāku liŋ nira mahā mamarīkṣa śakti*

saŋ rāmadéwa sira śūra sudhīra maṅsö,
taṅgap tikaŋ laras agöŋ maduluṙ tat aṅgwan,
śīghrāṙ watĕk ya kawĕnaŋ tumihaŋ tikaŋ hrū,
saŋ jāmadagni mawĕnĕs humĕnĕŋ kapūhan*

saŋ rāmabhāṙggawa Apanta tujuṅku liṅta,
yapwan gulūnta panahĕn yadiyan hatinta,
tan dadya nisphala Iké kita matya dèṅku,
yapwan palaṇḍuṅa manĕmbaha bhaktya sojar*

méraŋ siraŋ paraśurāma gĕlāna képwan,
trĕṣṇa sirèŋ hurip asiḥ wĕkasan ta mojar,
swaṙggāṅku dibya I ruhuṙ paṅahā hyaŋ indra,
yékāt panaḥ hilaṅakĕn mara tak para ṅkā*

nā liŋ niraŋ paraśurāma nĕhĕṙ ta luṅhā,
méraŋ tumona muka saŋ nrĕpapūtra rāma,
mahyā Ikaŋ bala kabèḥ nya humuŋ paḍātri,
saŋ mꜽtilī sira sahaṙṣa mariṙ makiṅkiŋ*

{mālinī}:2.78

atha ri sĕḍeŋ ikā saŋ bhāṙggawālaḥ ya luṅhā,
daśaratha sira haṙṣān kolakĕn pūtra rāma,
krama lumaku Umaṅkat tuṅgaṅan kapwa maṅrap,
satĕka nira sinuṅsuŋ dé nikaŋ wwaŋ ry ayodhyā#

#trĕtiyas saṙggaḥ#
<prĕthiwītala>:3.
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ : 17

dateŋ pwa maharāja saŋ daśaratha ry ayodhyāmpura,
inastuti ta saŋ naréndrasuta rāma dé niŋ sarāt,
apan Ilaṅakĕn musuḥ nira mahāṙṣi riŋ āśrama,
lawan paraśurāma śakti tuwi soṙ ataḥ dé nira*

tatan hana wanèḥ anuŋ pinuji dè nikaŋ wwaŋ kabèḥ,
naréndrasuta rāmadéwa sira śakti tātan kalèn,
amātya bhaṭamantri tuṣṭa magiraŋ paḍāṅastuti,
sirékana Iniṣṭi ratwa nikanāŋ ayodhyāpura*

samaṅkana naréndra saŋ daśarathāsi haṙṣāgiraŋ,
si rāma juga ratwa tan si bharata pwa na liŋ nira,
praśāsta karĕṅö parampara Ujaṙ naréndrāpagĕḥ,
samāpta winaraḥ tikaŋ bala kabéḥ ry ujaṙ saŋ prabhu*

anéka saji saṅgrahékaŋ abhiṣéka yomèḥ tĕkā,
sinaṅgraha sapādapāṭa maṇimukhya siṅhāsana,
lawan kanaka kumbha tīṙtha ya Isi nya sāmpun mawit,
ginomaya Ikaŋ sabhā sinawuran ta gandhākṣata*

sugandha kumukus ŋ Asöp ya tinatā kabèḥ tūt sisī,
kukus nya mawĕlun-wĕlun gugula dhūpa gandhotkaca,
sĕkaṙ surabhi cāmpakāsana sugandha lumrā marūm,
lawan dhwaja patāka komala kĕlab nya dé niŋ aṅin*

sĕḍĕŋ nira kināṙyya ratwaṅabhiṣéka yomèḥ tĕkā,
gĕlāna sira saŋ naréndraghariṇī siraŋ kékayī,
anak nira Ataḥ siraŋ bharata ratwa kahyun Ira,
apan pasamayan sĕḍĕŋ nira sinoma-somaḥ pwa wèḥ*

nda tan hana Anak nirāpara-paran maré saŋ kaki,
siraŋ bharata taṙ wĕruḥ ry aṅĕn-aṅĕn Iraŋ kékayī,
sirāta juga mogha kimburu tumon siraŋ rāghawa,
alaḥ pracaya riŋ-ŋ-ujaṙ samaya niŋ sumomaḥ sira*

masö sira ri saŋ narādhipa mahā mamighnāna don,
pininta nira saŋ naréndrasuta rāma muṅgèŋ alas,
anak nira Ataḥ ya ratwa kaharĕp niraŋ kékayī,
gĕlāna ta naréndra saŋ daśarathāśa képwan sira*

sawèt nikana satya saŋ prabhu kinon ŋ anak miṅgata,
kadi pwa ya Ilaŋ-ŋ asiḥ nira hiḍĕp nikaŋ wwaŋ kabéḥ,
gĕlāna maṅaraŋ ŋ-alaḥ salahasātimohāṅĕsaḥ,
mahöm ta sahana nya kapwa Umasö ri saŋ rāghawa*

aḥ-o lalu lalis naréndra tamatan panoliḥ guṇa,
lawan bharata duṣṭa hāḥ lalu gĕlĕḥ niraŋ kékayī,
nahan ya ta wuwus nya wĕḥ ri harèpan Iraŋ rāghawa,
tumūta Umarèŋ alas kira-kira nya tan kantuna*

sudhīra ta siraŋ nrĕpātmaja wawaŋ ta mojaṙ sira,
lakiṅku sahananta haywa malarāk parékāŋ alas,
apan Ikana Ājña saŋ prabhu Anugrahékin tĕka,
prayojana nikaŋ anak gumawayaŋ pakon iŋ bapa*

apan sira mamĕtwakĕn sira mawèḥ wruhèŋ loṙ kidul,
siréka maṅiṅū rumakṣa rikanāŋ anak riŋ bhaya,
agöŋ paṅupakāra saŋ prabhu mataŋ nya tag laṅghana,
lĕhöŋ mati misan-misan saka rikaŋ wihaŋ riŋ bapa*

tuliḥ ta sahananta haywa ta saśoka dé ni ṅhulun,
ariṅku ya siwinta saŋ bharata ratwa tan saṅśaya,
apan naku Ikāŋ ratuṇ ḍatu Ariṅku tātaṙ kalèn,
lawan sira naréndra taṅguhana haywa śoka ṅhati*

nahan Ikana liŋ nira krama madĕg ta luṅhā sira,
lawan Ari nirāta lakṣmaṇa tumūt siraŋ mꜽtilī,
sumantri mapatiḥ sirāṅatĕrakĕn parékāŋ alas,
lawan sahana saŋ sumādhya sira ratwa yāsiḥ tumūt*

ḍatĕŋ sira rikāŋ alas ri tamasā mahārāmya-ya,
lalu ŋ diwasa maṅhinĕp sira rikāŋ alas bhīṣaṇa,
rinākṣa nira tékanaŋ bala kabèḥ pijeṙ yāturū,
waṅuṇ ḍahina śīghra miṅgat aṅĕnĕs ta saŋ rāghawa*

siraŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇāmilu lawan siraŋ mꜽthilī,
tatan hana wĕruḥ sĕḍĕŋ niran umiṅgat aṅlĕs hilaŋ,
gĕlāna Ikanaŋ balān pawuṅu lèn sumantryāṅaraŋ,
apan kahilaṅan taman wruḥ i wĕkas niraŋ rāghawa*

humuŋ ya manaṅis rikāŋ alas alaḥ masāmbat masū,
ṭatan wruḥ i pamètana nya ri siraŋ hilaŋ tan katon,
maluy ta ya kabèḥ muliḥ tĕka rikĕŋ ayodhyāpura,
manaḥ nya juga tan muliḥ milu tumūt risaŋ rāghawa*

lawan saŋ apatiḥ sumantri marahup sirèŋ lwaḥ magöŋ,
linālana niraŋ manaḥ makin agöŋ ta kiṅkiŋ nira,
muliḥ ta sira tūt hawan r-aṅĕn-aṅen ta saŋ rāghawa,
ḍatĕŋ sira rikāŋ ayodhyapura śūnya taŋ rāt hiḍĕp*

masuk sira rikaŋ kaḍatwan umasö ri saŋ bhūpati,
mulat pwa naranātha saŋ daśarathāṅaraŋ mūṙcchita,
apan mulat i saŋ sumantri juga taṙ parowaŋ sira,
tĕñuḥ hati nirāpasaḥ r-aṅĕn-aṅĕn lara niŋ anak*

inastuti sirèŋ daṅū pinuji dhīra tātaṙ lĕgö,
sahiṣṇu humĕnĕŋ kumĕlakĕn ikaŋ larāgöŋ tĕmĕn,
mĕné ri papasaḥ nira pwa ya sahiṣṇu tātan hana,
gupé kapalupuy hiḍĕp nira hilaŋ kadhīran nira*

sĕkul taṙ aharĕp Asiŋ sarumakĕt tuwīn āryakĕn,
mariṙ pawĕḍihan malit Inalapan tikaŋ bhūṣaṇa,
mahas mabayaṅan manaḥ nira n-akūŋ kinuṅkuŋ juga,
nahan laku marèŋ taman sira lumālanékaŋ manaḥ*

makin pwa ya makūŋ ikaŋ hati gĕlāna monĕŋ ataḥ,
naréndra baribin manaḥ nira tumon taman rāmya-ya,
waliŋ nira paṅoṣadhān lumipurāŋ unĕŋ riŋ anak,
muliḥ sira sakèŋ taman malara kaṣṭa puḥ mūṙcchita*

hanan kĕlu rikaŋ tilām tuwi malit malĕmbut matīs,
awak nira linépanèŋ suluṙ usĕṙ lawan caṇḍana,
nda tan paraṣa tan panīsi mapanas kabèḥ yan hiḍĕp,
ri tībra nikanāŋ unĕŋ dadi muliḥ sirèŋ swaṙgga wèḥ*

mawū mawalikan n-anākĕbi niraŋ naréndrānaṅis,
gĕluŋ linuputan Apus nya Umuré sawèt niŋ lara,
maṇik kanaka bhūṣaṇādi sĕsĕran tibā riŋ lĕmaḥ,
apan maguliṅan gĕlāna makuśā masāmbat masū*

amātya bhaṭamantri kapwa ta masö mahöm-höm kabèḥ,
siraŋ bharata śīghra yaṙ laku muliḥ hinundaŋ ḍatĕŋ,
tinon ira tikaŋ kaḍatwan asamun ya tistis kabèḥ,
kadi pwa lĕburékanaŋ lĕbuḥ apan tayāŋ dwal mĕtu*

sagadgada manaḥ niraṙ laku masuk riŋ abhyantara,
umuŋ sahana saŋ kapaṅguḥ anaṅis sumuṅsuŋ sira,
matakwan amĕpeṙ siré kalara saŋ naréndrāṙ pĕjaḥ,
satorasi sirāŋ ibū marahakĕn siré saŋ anak*

huwus nira wĕruḥ ri hétu nira saŋ naréndrāṙ pĕjaḥ,
saroṣa magĕlĕŋ sirèŋ ibu masö ta mojaṙ sira,
lukan kita harébu niṙ-ghrĕṇa hatinta duṣṭāgĕlĕḥ,
wĕnaŋ kita rumuddha kāṙyya naranātha tātaṙ hĕnĕŋ*

apa k-phala ri saŋ tigāṙ para rikāŋ alas duṙggama,
kitat hana rikāŋ ayodhya pira göṅa nīnakta wèḥ,
kunaŋ kami kabèḥ umilwa mati dènta wèt niŋ lara,
aḥ-o saphala dènta māmbĕk umatīŋ sarāt taṙ masiḥ*

Ṅhulun niki kinonta ratwa Aparan guṇā niŋ ratu,
yadin pamuharā wirodha Umalākĕnaŋ rāt kabèḥ,
lawan-n-aku winèḥta sora Adhamā sakèŋ lakṣmaṇa,
tumūt ya drĕḍabhakti tāṙ alaŋ-alaŋ ri saŋ rāghawa*

nahan nikana liŋ nirāṅuman-uman ri saŋ kékayī,
tataṙ gĕrĕmĕ ratwa dhīra sira satya bhaktīŋ kaka,
nirantara humīs ta luḥ nira gĕlāna wèt niŋ lara,
wawaŋ sira kataṅguhan maṅĕn-aṅĕn pĕjaḥ saŋ prabhu*

sinantwa sira dé nikaŋ bala kabèḥ lawan saŋ ibu,
ilaŋ lara nirālilaŋ hati maho maluy niṙmmala,
apan prakrĕti jāti niŋ dadi kabèḥ matuṅtuŋ pati,
ya tékan inaṅĕn-aṅĕn Ira hilaŋ ta kiṅkiŋ nira*

kinon ira ta saŋ balādhika tumunwa saŋ bhūpati,
maśoca ta mawèḥ tilĕm sira rikaŋ tilem niŋ wulan,
samāpta maharèp ta saŋ bharata mèta saŋ rāghawa,
ri satya nira bhakti riŋ kaka tirun nikaŋ rāt kabĕḥ*

liman kuda lawan ratha pramuka niŋ balānuŋ tumūt,
sĕnaddha dumuluṙ siraŋ bharata śīghra luṅhā sira,
tĕka pwa sira riŋ alas gaja rathāśwa kapwānusup,
mahas sira rikāŋ alas Umulisāk ri saŋ rāghawa*

ri piṅgiṙ ikanaŋ nadī ri tamasérikā duṙggama,
alas gahana gahwarāgraha guhā nya gambhīra ya,
lawan kali juraŋ trĕbis biṣama bhīṣaṇālwāṅawit,
siraŋ bharata tātakut nira Alaḥ Umèt saŋ kaka*

taman katĕmu saŋ pinèt lumaku saŋ mamèt taṙ maṅèl,
tĕmu ŋ lwaḥ atiniṙmmalātiśaya dibya gaṅgā gahan,
maṇik sphaṭika candrakāṇṭa ya paḍa nya śuddhāputiḥ,
kadi pwa ya manaḥ niraŋ bharata satya bhaktīŋ kaka*

muwaḥ ta manusup rikān katĕmu tékanaŋ lwaḥ magöŋ,
pratīta yamunā ṅaranya makiris hilī nyāhĕniŋ,
i soṙ hana ta saṅgama nya kalawan ta gaṅgāputiḥ,
kadi pwa ya bhaṭāra wiṣṇu kalawan bhaṭāréśwara*

muwaḥ ta manusup hana pwa patapan pinaṅguḥ nira,
subhikṣa ya manoharāśrama niraŋ bharadwāja ya,
sĕḍĕŋ tiba-tibāṅlaluŋ diwasa kāla soré n tĕka,
mahāṙṣi saha śisya gorawa masö manuṅsuŋ sira*

anéka panamuy mahāṙṣi mĕtu saṅka riŋ yoga ya,
amogha manurun manojña kayu pārijātādbhuta,
asiŋ sakaharĕp saménaka pawèḥ niraŋ paṇḍita,
aho saphala niŋ tapātiśaya saṙwwakāmaprada*

anākĕbi riŋ indraloka manurun lawan Apsarī,
ya téka makurĕn-kuren ri sira saŋ tamuy kādbhuta,
mabaṅsi maṅiduŋ makinnara malāwu wīṇāṅigĕl,
jĕnĕk ta sira saŋ tamuy dadi tĕhĕṙ maṅantyaṅhinĕp*

waṅuṇ ḍahina śīghra yaṙ laku muwaḥ umèt saŋ kaka,
lawan bala ḍatĕŋ sirèŋ talaga dibya mandākinī,
kathañcana hana pwa nagna wanawāsa paṅguḥ nira,
siromarahakĕn pradéśa kahanan niraŋ rāghawa*

pawitra hana citrakūṭagiri duṙggamāwān magöŋ,
manohara ya rāmya yéka kahanan niraŋ rāghawa,
sahaṙṣa winaraḥ ta saŋ bharata śīghra maṅkat sira,
lawan bala kabèḥ manèk sira rikaŋ gunuŋ duṙggama*

umèḥ nira tĕkā sasaṅśaya mulat ta saŋ lakṣmaṇa,
waliŋ nira musuḥ ḍatĕŋ r-adĕgakĕn ta laṅkap nira,
sĕnaddha pinasuk niraŋ kawaca yatna dhīrāṅadĕg,
alis nira ya cāla mārĕṅu lalāṭa kumrūkĕna*

tinon ira ya taṙ pasañjata taya ŋ galaḥ tāpapan,
tuhun kuda liman rathādulu-duluṙ ya makwèḥ juga*
makin ta maparö wĕruḥ siran inaryakĕn taŋ laras,
masö sira ri saŋ kakāwara-waraḥ ri saŋ rāghawa*

siraŋ bharata śīghra yaṙ tĕka masö manambaḥ sira,
lawan bala nirāwaraḥ ta sira yaṙ pĕjaḥ saŋ prabhu,
saśoka manaṅis humuŋ sira kabèḥ sawèt niŋ lara,
anantara mariṙ makiṅkiŋ arahup ta madyus kabèḥ*

naréndrasuta rāma sāmpun arahup ta mojaṙ sira,
ariṅku bharatāt uliḥ hara rikaŋ ayodhyāpura,
ujaṙ haji Ikā dumèḥ aku marèŋ alas tan kalèn,
kitékana gumantya ratwa ya mataŋ nya tat saṅśayā*

lawan kita magöŋ guṇanta gaṇitan tatan hĕntya-ya,
prawīra wihikan kitèŋ aji lawan kalap niŋ naya,
mataŋ nya kita yogya ratwa saphalān siwin rākṣakā,
guṇanta Aparan guṇa nya yadi tan guṇa niŋ ratu*

kunĕŋ yan alĕmĕḥ pi ratwa ri hanaṅku muṅgwiŋ alas,
ujaṙku pituhunta kéwala kitāta bhaktyākaka,
awās ya mulihāta liṅku kita haywa śoka ṅhati,
hanā ta juga rākṣakā kita rikaŋ kaḍatwan Ari*

nahan ya ta wuwus nirātiśaya dhīra dibyaŋ manaḥ,
wĕnaŋ nira rumākṣa saŋ bapa rikā kasatyan Ira,
samaṅkana siraŋ kinon muliha ratwa tātan lĕgö,
siraŋ bharata bhakti riŋ kaka wawaŋ ta mojaṙ sira*

pirā Inaka ni ṅhulun hana rikaŋ kaḍatwan kunĕŋ,
sĕḍĕṅta humiḍĕp Ikaŋ lara hanèŋ alas kāsyasiḥ,
lawan kita ta yogya ratwa tuwi rākṣakā niŋ jagat,
apan matuha śaktimānta guṇamānta śūrèŋ raṇa*

nya taŋ kuda liman lawan kanaka ratna yogya prabhu,
ndya yuktyan ikihĕn ṅhulun kumawaśākĕnékā kabèḥ,
amītya bhaṭamantri yogya karikā sumiwya ṅhulun,
mataŋ nya mulihāta ménaka kitāta bhūpālaka*

lawan ṅhulun atīta niṙgguṇa guṇanta gaṅgopama,
diwākara gunuŋ paḍanta himawān lawan sāgara,
ṅhulun pwa pinujinta śakti guṇamānta tātan tuhu,
asambhawa wuwusta maṅduhuṅakĕn mahā maṅlaré#

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}:3.52
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ : 15

nahan ikana wuwus saŋ kékayīputra sādhu,
dadi sumahuṙ ikā saŋ rāmabhadrāsi maswī,
muliha Ata kitāntĕn ṅkā ry ayodhyā tamolaḥ,
yadin alĕmĕha séwan pādukaṅkwīki ratwa#

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}:3.53

ndan kita pi sarabhāran rākṣaŋ sakala jagat,
kṣatriyawinayā yékā rākṣan katuturakĕn,
śāsaṇa ya gĕgĕn taŋ śāstra d-wulati lanā,
sojariŋ aji tūtĕn yékā mawa kasukan*

dèwa kuśala śālā mwaŋ dhaṙmma ya pahayun,
mās ya ta pahawrĕddhin byāyā riŋ hayu kĕkĕsĕn,
bhukti sakaharĕptād wèhi ŋ bala kasukan,
dhaṙmma kalawan aṙtha mwaŋ kāmāta ṅaran ikā*

Śīla rahayu rākṣan rāga dwéśa hilaṅakĕn,
kimburu ya ta hīlan śūnyāmbĕkta lawan awak,
nyāŋ winaya gĕgön asiŋ solaḥ kinalulutan,
mwaŋ abhimana sampat antĕnku prabhu maṅaliḥ*

wruḥ pwa kita rikāṅdé prajñā dibya ṅaran ikā,
riŋ raṇamuka sāra mwaŋ wākśūra ya guṇitan,
tyāga kita mapuṇyā riŋ brahmāṅśa muniwara,
nāgata gawayĕntāt rākṣāŋ rāt ya pahapagĕḥ#

{rucira}:3.56
⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ : 13

krĕtajñatā haran ikanaŋ wruḥ iŋ guṇa,
mulat rikaŋ bala manĕkĕt manon ulaḥ,
asiŋ lèwiḥ linĕwihakĕn rikaŋ hayu,
ikaŋ masoṙ kinila-kilèŋ sasambhawa*

mahāt-manon guṇagaṇa dibya riŋ prabhu,
tumon ikaŋ hala-hayu yatna tan hĕnĕŋ,
rumĕṅwaken lara nikanaŋ prajā kabèḥ,
apan Ikāŋ ubhaga lanā ri saŋ prabhu#

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}:3.59
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ : 8

utsāhāta larapana,
kāṙyyāsiŋ pahapagĕhĕn,
sampay tan gawayakĕna,
riŋ satwādhama ya tuwi*

Śaktī siṅha katatakut,
riŋ wīrāsama winuwus,
yatnā nyān pamati-mati,
yékānuŋ satiru-tirun*

göŋ hĕṅkāra ya ta hilan,
nindā tan gawayakĕna,
tañ janmāmuhara wĕrö,
yékā praśraya sumuka#

{pawitrā}:3.62
– – – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ : 9

nyāŋ mukyāntĕn kanĕkĕtakĕn,
haywāsampay riŋ asiḥ-asiḥ,
dibyaŋ śāstrān linagi-lagin,
yāwat mèwĕḥ ya pinituhun*

saṅka niŋ wruḥ aji ginĕgö,
nītijñācāra kapuhara,
paṇḍyācāṙyya dwija pahayun,
göṅĕntātaḥ ikanaŋ asiḥ*

krodhāmbĕk yélagakèn ika,
doṣākwèḥ duṙbbala winuwus,
mwaŋ wadwānuŋ rahayu milag,
mitrādoḥ taŋ musuḥ aparĕk*

śāntāsiḥ nitya tuhagaṇan,
haywāpĕs riŋ kinatakutan,
wadwā doṣa nya palĕ-palĕḥ,
tan wruḥ riŋ twaŋ ya guragaḍa*

kadyaṅgā niŋ wèḍus upaman,
bhītātwaŋ riŋ kayu maṅadĕg,
yapwan suṇḍé wijaḥ umanèk,
Īchā tan saṅśaya malayū*

doṣāgöŋ wwaŋ jenĕk aṅinum,
māhā ŋ cittālupa mawĕrö*
pāruṣyèŋ wwaŋ prakaṭa wĕgig,
rāhasyāsiŋ winuni mĕtu*

haywādwa-dwāmuhara hala,
duṙbhāgāwās ta ya Inupĕt,
mwaŋ wadwāsiŋ kuṭila katon,
tan wiśwāsāna ta Ikahen*

nindā riŋ wwaŋ ya ta manapis,
tan saktā riŋ wiṣaya dahat,
dyūtāsiŋ duṙyyasana kunĕŋ,
yékānuŋ tan gawayakĕna#

{prĕthiwītala}:3.70
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ ⏓ : 17

nihan ta gawayanta nitya maṅĕmit prajā maṇḍala,
wihāra pahayunta paṙhyaṅan umaḥ bhaṭārāmĕrĕn,
hawan patani pañcuran talaga sétu tambak taman,
pĕkĕn wwatan asiŋ sakahyuna nikaŋ prajā yad-gawé*

limanta ratha tuṅgaṅan lagi-lagin śraman sañjata,
mawèha kita kaṙmma piṇḍa rĕṣibhojanāṅkĕn salèk,
ikaŋ kuśala hosakĕnta ya kabèḥ pamūjā gĕṅĕn,
ya tonĕn ikanaŋ sarāt kita janānurāgérikā*

wulatta rikanaŋ manéwita kabèḥ watĕk séwaka,
guṇa nya kalawan Asiḥnya matuhan Ikā tiṅhali,
suśīla saguṇātibhakti yadi tan sujanmā tuwi,
sayogya pahayun Ikā ṅuni-ṅunin sujanmālapĕn*

tatan wawaŋ awèha riŋ suka parīkṣanĕntériya,
lumakwakĕna ŋ ajña yan dadi rikā ta yan wèhana,
guṇa nya mapagĕḥ manaḥ nika sumiwya saŋ bhūpati,
kitékana kināsihan subhaga dibya ratnopama*

samaṅkana Ikaŋ manéwita yadin salobhāsulit,
hanomarahakĕn ya tan rahayu lāgi saṅkĕŋ hala,
iṅetakĕna cāra yékana paṅawruhèŋ duṙjjana,
asiŋ lagi katon bĕnĕṙ nya-ya ta gopitan saŋ prabhu*

awās ya hala wigrahanta Ika yan Ulaḥ nyān salaḥ,
hilāṅakĕna yan sadoṣa wuwusĕn wiwékan tĕmĕn,
samaṅkana yadin r-ahat dĕmakananta wèhĕn suka,
ya tékana wĕnaŋ anugraha lawan wĕnaŋ wigraha*

bhaṭāra rawi yopamanta manasèŋ sarāt taṙ maṅèl,
samaṅkana ta saŋ prabhūmilaṅakĕn Ikaŋ duṙjjana,
śaśaṅka magawé Asiḥ sira janānurāgèŋ sarāt,
awās ta kita maṅkanāri yat ahāta riŋ pun-punan*

gunuŋ ya ta paḍanta bhūpati Ikaŋ prajāṅkĕn ḍukut,
patūti guṇa-doṣa niŋ ulaḥ ikā mataŋ nyān suka,
ikaŋ prawara pora waṙgga wanatulya yāṅkĕn Alas,
kitékana ta siṅha rākṣaka dumèḥ nya śobhān katon#

{Śikhariṇī}:3.78
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ : 17

ikaŋ thāni prītīnubhaya guṇa niŋ bhūpati lanā,
ya saṅka nyāŋ bhogān hana pakĕna niŋ rājya ya tuwi,
asiŋ sénāluḥ nyékana ta tuluṅĕn haywa humĕnĕŋ,
lima lwiṙ niŋ sākṣāt bhaya tĕka rikaŋ pora ya paḍĕm*

kinonkon saŋ swāmīkana ta Umarèŋ wanwa mapanas,
maliŋ makwèḥ lumrāṅhala-hala lawan drohaka wanèḥ,
kapāt nyékā saŋ wallabha ya winilaŋ duṣṭa tan alaḥ,
lima mwaŋ lobhé saŋ narapati nahan nyaŋ bhaya magöŋ*

mataŋ nyāntĕn tiṅhal sahana ni watĕk niŋ bala dĕlön,
ikaŋ prajña wruḥ riŋ naya winaya śīla nya rahayu,
tan alwāmwaŋ yatnān drĕḍa maniwi tan lobha samatā,
nahan pratyakṣantèŋ hala-hayu taman dadya manasar*

sunītī priḥ tāntĕn gagapi hati göṅĕn guṇagaṇan,
musuḥ topāyan toḥ pisani panas iŋ pāśa pahasat,
iké śatruntad-don sahana pakĕna mwaŋ kira-kira,
tatan wèhĕntātābhawaha gĕsĕṅiŋ drohaka raraḥ*

ikaŋ mèṅĕt wruḥ nyèŋ maniwi mulat iŋ bhakti ya gawé,
prayatna wruḥ riŋ dé tan alĕmĕha riŋ krĕtya rahayu,
wĕrö niŋ cittāgöŋ ya ta hilaṅakĕn riŋ hati lagé,
swabhāwèŋ janmékaŋ mada kaluṣa tātaḥ ya manaput*

kaśaktin mwaŋ prajña kuśala ya ta bhoga nya tamalaḥ,
surūpā tatwajñèŋ aji ya sapujintékana kabèḥ,
kitāntĕn saṅkĕp riŋ guṇagaṇa Ikaŋ bhakti sudrĕḍa,
hilantékāŋ ambĕk manaya-naya mattāmiṣa puji*

nahan dé saŋ nāthākĕmita Irikaŋ bhūmi subhaga,
parāṙthāsiḥ yāgöŋ saka lara nikaŋ rāt winulatan,
tumiṅhal yātāsiŋ sawuwus ikanāŋ śāsana tinūt,
tepĕt māsiḥ taṙ wruḥ kutila milag iŋ bañcana dumĕḥ*

{Śikhariṇī}:3.78
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ : 17

nahan tojaṙ saŋ rāma manĕkĕt iŋ antĕn mapagĕha,
sahaṙṣāmbĕk saŋ bhārata-ta rumĕṅö śabda karuṇa,
manĕmbaḥ māmwīt saŋ bharata ri siraŋ rāmawijaya,
lawan wadwākwèḥ mwaŋ sahana-hana niŋ bhrĕtya mamuhun*

{tiḍak ḍikĕtahui}:3.86
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ : 15

tinawanakĕn irékaŋ pādukātyanta dibya,
ya ta siniwi sinĕmbaḥ dé nikaŋ wwaŋ ry ayodhyā,
bharata sira tamolaḥ bhakti maṅrākṣa rājya#

#catuṙthas saṙggaḥ#
<mālabhāriṇi>:4.1
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ : 11
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏓ : 12

ndat atīta sirāṙ hanèŋ kaḍatwan,
sira saŋ rāma hanèŋ alas tāmolaḥ,
rikanaŋ giri citrakūṭa r-uṅgu,
kalawan lakṣmaṇa jānakī sūsatya*

hana tāśrama saŋ mahāṙṣi Atri,
ya tikānuŋ pinaran niraŋ tīgaŋ wwaŋ,
atigorawa saŋ mahāṙṣi maṅliŋ,
karuṇékaŋ śaraṇāgatātīdibya*

tamataṙ malawas sirāṙ hana ṅka,
hana tālas karĕṅö pratīta riŋ lwā,
atibhīṣaṇa daṇḍakā ṅaranya,
ya paran saŋ raghuputra rāmādéwa*

{prabodhitā}:4.4
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓  : 11
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ : 11

umahas sira ta hanaŋ katākut,
kalawan saŋ ari lèn priyā nira,
hana rākṣasa rodra yéka maṅsö,
umahā mātyana donya tan kalèn*

{mālabhāriṇi}:4.5
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ : 11
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ : 12

si wirādha ṅaranya tan panoli,
i ruhuṙ n-uṅgu suku nya wèḥ sumuṅsaŋ,
atirodra taṅanya paṅlaku nya,
atakut mrĕtyu tumon ya rodrarūpa*

umulat ta naréndraputra kāliḥ,
sira tātaṙ matakut masö tumandaŋ,
awamāna Ikaŋ wirādha mūṙkka,
tumahā saŋ nrĕpaputra hīnaśakti*

umasö ta maṅaŋ tutuk nya malwa,
kadi raṇḍö ta suku nya bhinna yāgöŋ,
maluṅid kadi gañjiran kuku nya,
ya ta paṅduk nya ri saŋ naréndraputra*

umulat sira kā-rwa śīghra maṅsö,
sumikĕp kā-rwa matuṅgalan suku nya,
sinĕbit wadi dé nirāṙ dudut ya,
mati tātan pabiṣān śiwak k-awak nya*

ri pĕjaḥ nikanaŋ wirādha mūṙkka,
umahas saŋ nrĕpaputra niṙbhayātaḥ,
tĕmu ŋ āśrama dibya śoba rāmya,
patapan saŋ Śarabhaṅga yoga siddhi*

sira saŋ rĕṣi siddha dibya yogī,
wihikan riŋ paramāṙtha tatwa sūkṣma,
paripakwa samādhi niṣkalĕṅka,
dadi mamwit ta siromarèŋ kamokṣan*

kita rāma ṅaranta rājaputra,
kami mamwīta marérikaŋ kamokṣan,
lalu bhāgya tĕmĕn kitāt para ṅké,
kita nārāyaṇa maṅgalaṅku dibya*

hana tāśrama saŋ sutīkṣṇa yogī,
yatikānuŋ wĕgilĕnta tat makūṅa,
maparö ya taman madoḥ saṅka ṅké,
rĕṣi yogī śaraṇānta saŋ sutīkṣṇa*

iti nā ta wuwus niraŋ tapaswī,
dadi tāyoga sirāsamādhi siddhi,
magawé ta sira bahnīdharāṇa,
magĕsöŋ śīṙṇna Awak nirātma pāsaḥ*

atha mokṣa siraŋ mahāṙṣi siddhi,
kawĕkas saŋ raghuputra rāmadéwa,
umuwaḥ manusup sirèŋ alas göŋ,
tĕmu tékāśrama saŋ sutīkṣṇa yogī*

saphalān winĕgil siraŋ sutīkṣṇa,
karuṇā riŋ wanawāsakācithī ya,
malawas ta naréndraputra rāma,
rikanāŋ āśrama wèt nyasiḥ mahāṙṣi*

{prabodhitā}:4.16
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ : 10
⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ : 11

umahas ta sirèŋ tapowana,
tinamuy dé nira saŋ mahāmuni,
phalamūla pawĕḥ niraŋ rĕṣi,
yatikāhāra nirāṙ hanèŋ alas*

i sĕḍĕŋ nikanaŋ wĕṅin tĕka,
maturū saŋ nrĕpaputra riŋ ŋ-alas,
kalaśā nira ron ikaŋ kayu,
umahā mabrata dhīra taṙ lĕgö*

rahina nya mahas sirèŋ alas,
mrĕga yā téka gawé nirāburu,
mamatīka kĕnas rikĕŋ alas,
ya pamūjā nira nityakāla ya*

wiku paṇḍita wédapāraga,
umahas māmĕŋ-amĕŋ riŋ āśrama,
rasikā tinamuy ya dé nira,
pinakāhāra saśéṣa saŋ tamuy*

wiku rūpa nirāṙ hanèŋ alas,
paḍa santoṣa rikaŋ kulit kayu,
kayu yéka kadaŋ nirādasiḥ,
ya paṅhöban nira kāla niŋ panas*

sira tāpasawéṣa yan katon,
ndan ikāŋ āyudha yéka tan kasaḥ,
abhayā nira saŋ mahāṙṣi don,
brata saŋ wīra rumākṣa saŋ wiku*

patapan ri samīpa niŋ gunuŋ,
paḍa kapwénahasan ta dé nira,
kinĕmit ya rinākṣa riŋ bhaya,
suka ménak ta pahoma saŋ rĕṣi*

salawas niraṙ uṅgu riŋ ŋ-alas,
tamatan lèn inaṅĕn-aṅĕn Ira,
suka duḥka niraŋ mahāmuni,
ya cinitta winiwéka riŋ hati*

saphalāṙ wĕka saŋ raghūttama,
ikanaŋ citta parāṙtha kéwala,
taṙ upékṣa lara nyawak nira,
prihataḥ kāṙyya niraŋ mahāmuni*

kramakāla Umèḥ kulĕm tĕkā,
rikanāŋ āśrama sāndhyawéla ya,
tamataṙ malupèŋ bratājapa,
kadi saŋ tāpa susatya sātwika*

rahina nya Atīta taŋ kulĕm,
sakatambé Umuwaḥ sirājapa,
tamataṙ kalupan hĕlĕm-hĕlĕm,
matutuṙ tèŋ brata dhīra niścala*

hana Śūṙppaṇakhā ta rākṣasī,
ya tikā cāra niraŋ daśānana,
umahas ya rikāŋ alas kabèḥ,
tĕka riŋ daṇḍaka kānanāśrama*

tinĕmu nya ta saŋ nrĕpātmaja,
riŋ alas kāwit amèt sĕkaṙ sira,
kalawan janakātmajādulur,
sira taṙ kāntun asiŋ paran tumūt*

dadi mūṙ ya tumon sirādulur,
ikanaŋ Śūṙppaṇakā ta kéraṅan,
manusup ya rikāŋ alas wanèḥ,
tĕmu saŋ lakṣmaṇa tāṅalap sĕkar*

kĕna kāma sarāga yan wulat,
magawé bhāwa mahiñji yan laku,
paripūṙṇna Awak nya riŋ hayu,
wulan iŋ puṙṇnamakāla tulya ya#

{mālabhāriṇi}:4.31
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ : 11

maḍĕmit sapĕgĕg tĕṅaḥ nya māmbĕt,
mamanis lèn pamata nya rāmya molĕm,
malurus ta pupū nya lén wĕtis nya,
jariji nyānuji laṇḍak ujwalābāŋ*

jaghana nya magöŋ susu nya buntĕr,
maputiḥ huntwalaris Iruŋ nya śobhā,
sĕsĕranya maṇik manojña saśrī,
masĕkaṙ rāmya marumpukan masumpiŋ*

mamanis ta wulat nya lèn guyu nya,
ikana lwiṙ nya makin sarāga mahyun,
ri sawèt ni hiyunya tā Iraŋ nya,
ri siraŋ lakṣmaṇa yan masö ta mojar*

kaka lakṣmaṇa hé sumitraputra,
aku mūṙcchā kĕna kāma dènta tibra,
asihanta kunĕŋ taman pahīṅan,
hulunantāku baśā kité tuwuḥku*

salawas ni huripku tan kasāha,
ri kitāsiŋ saparanta tan madoha,
sapakonta riké ṅhulun kadadya,
ri sĕḍĕṅtāt anumāna riŋ kĕnèŋ hyun*

iti nā ta wuwus nya tā Iraŋ nya,
sinaput dé ni panaḥ bhaṭāra kāma,
sumahuṙ ta siraŋ sinoma-somaḥ,
sira saŋ lakṣmaṇa gadgada ta dé nya*

aparan kita dibyarūpa mojar,
ry apa saṅkanta Amānuṣākrĕtinta,
tamatat matakut rikèŋ alas göŋ,
tak anon ŋ-waŋ tuwi lèn anuŋ tĕka ṅké*

lalu dibya hayunta kādbhutāku,
apa jātinta yan apsarī ta kūnĕŋ,
paricāra ta wīnèḥ ya kantūna,
kita kanyāhayu towi tuṅga-tuṅgal*

{prabodhitā}:4.39
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏓ : 10

nya dumèḥ aku saṅśayā tĕmĕn,
kita mojaṙ ry aku tan kĕnèŋ iraŋ,
kadi mèdi wuwusta maṅlaré,
kita déwākrĕti mānuṣa ṅhulun*

yuwatī kita kanyakā kunĕŋ,
adhawātaḥ lakunta ta diṇḍarā,
ya mataŋ nya taman kĕnèŋ iraŋ,
ta wuwus torasi ri ṅhulun-n-ari*

kalawan-n-aku tak sayogya wèḥ,
ri kakaṅku t-para yogya māsiha,
sira rāma ṅaran nirèŋ jagat,
anumānèŋ kĕna rāga mūṙcchita*

guṇamānta sĕḍĕṅta yowana,
sira saŋ rāma ta māsihé kita,
wihikan maṅiriŋ ŋ-anakkĕbi,
sira tāmolya ri kahyunanta wèḥ*

amanis pamata-n-nirālaris,
paṅawak sahya lawan mukābuṅaḥ,
tuwi bāhu nirāwiḍaŋ katon,
paṅalaḥ śatru gawé nya riŋ raṇa*

hana kadga nirātitīkṣṇa ya,
tan adoḥ yadyapi yan tĕkāŋ musuḥ,
tinahā Ikanaŋ raṇān tĕkā,
ya karākṣā nira don ikaŋ tĕwĕk*

wwara tāyudha lèn laras magöŋ,
taya tāŋ wwaŋ umĕnaŋ mayat tikā,
paṅalaḥ nira riŋ musuḥ kabèḥ,
ikanaŋ rākṣasa mūṙkka sāhasa*

sumukū patapan mahāmuni,
hana mighnékana yajña saŋ rĕṣi,
rĕṣiśatru ya mélik iŋ wiku,
ya pinatyan n-ira tan paśéṣa ya*

suka saŋ rĕṣi niṙbhayĕŋ alas,
ri kadibyan niraŋ āṙyya rāghawa,
ya mataŋ nya sayogya yat siwin,
kita bhāgyan yadiyat paré sira*

wara lakṣmaṇa nā ta liŋ nira,
ikanaŋ Śūṙppaṇakhā gĕlāna ya,
rumĕṅö guṇa saŋ raghūttama,
dadi maṅsö ya sahaṙṣa yan tĕka*

satĕka nya wuwus nya tan kalèn,
sira saŋ rāma wawaŋ sirāsahur,
ari dibya hayunta komala,
lalu hémanta ya tan kataṅgapa*

nya sirāri Ariṅku taṙ madoḥ,
sira sītā karĕṅö rikĕŋ sarāt,
tamatak maṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn wanèḥ,
rasikā tuṅgal ataḥ kurĕnkwari*

nya kunĕŋ wuwusaṅkwi yogya ya,
ikanāriṅku si lakṣmaṇāt para,
kurĕna nya kitāri māsiha,
kita kanyā ta surūpa komala*

raghuputra nahan wuwus nira,
ikanaŋ Śūṙppaṇakhā maluy ta ya,
i siraŋ taruṇāṙyya lakṣmaṇa,
alaḥ ahyun kĕna kāmabāṇa ya*

umasö ta taman kĕnèŋ iraŋ,
sumĕḍĕk kéraŋ-iraŋ ulaḥ nya wèḥ,
tan ulaḥ nikanāŋ anakkĕbi,
pinakolaḥ nya ya nīca kaśmala*

umulat maṅiṅĕt-iṅĕtakĕn,
sira saŋ lakṣmaṇa kādbhutaŋ manaḥ,
kala mūṙkka Iké ta rākṣasī,
ya ta sandéha sirāṙ sikĕp ta ya*

tinĕwöṙ nira nāsikā niké,
ikanéruŋ nya huwus pĕgat hilaŋ,
umĕsat ya mibĕṙ marèŋ laṅit,
mĕtu jāti nya-ya rākṣasīn katon*

aku Śūṙppaṇakhāku rākṣasī,
kita tan wruḥ ry aku mūḍa kāsyasiḥ,
jaga yatna huripta rākṣa ya,
biṣamāt mātya tka kākaṅku śighra*

khara dūṣaṇa rakṣasottama,
rikanaŋ śākti paḍa nya tan hana,
aniwāṙyya-ya wīra riŋ raṇa,
kita kāliḥ uliha nya yan tĕkā*

ri huwus ni wuwus nya maṅgĕmĕr,
malayū Śūṙppaṇakhānaṅis ta ya,
winĕgil nya kaka nya śīghra ya,
triśiraḥ mwaŋ kara lèn si dūṣaṇa*

kaka hé triśiraḥ tuluŋ ṅhulun,
lalu tad wruḥ ri laraṅku mohita,
tamatan paṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn kita,
ikanaŋ śatru ya sāhasé ṅhulun*

wwara rāma ṅaranya tāpasa,
hana tāri nya ṅaranya lakṣmaṇa,
wikubhāwa katon mahāṙddhika,
gumĕgö ŋ āyudha duṣṭacitta ya*

paribhūta wĕnaŋ ya sāhasa,
tumĕwöṙ téka Iruṅku niṙghrĕṇa,
tuwi tan hana doṣa ni ṅhulun,
ikanaŋ lakṣmaṇa yomahāwĕgig*

yadiyat hĕnĕṅāta riŋ musuḥ,
tat asĕṅhit hana sāhasé ṅhulun,
apa dona ni jīwitaṅku wèḥ,
apa tak péruŋ iraṅku tan sipi*

prabhu rāwaṇa nātha ni ṅhulun,
tuwi makwèḥ ta kakaṅku rākṣasa,
tamataṙ matakut t-ikaŋ musuḥ,
ya masampé ry aku tan pakāraṇa*

aparan ta guṇaṅku yak hanā,
lĕhĕṅaŋ mātya kunĕŋ misan-misan,
yadiyat hĕnĕṅāta riŋ musuḥ,
tat asĕṅhit hana sāhasé ṅhulun*

{mālabhāriṇi}:4.65

ya mataŋ nya yadin hanāsihanta,
ikanaŋ rāghawa lakṣmaṇolihanta,
aku niśśaraṇā kitāśrayaṅkwa,
yan agöŋ śakti nikaŋ musuḥ prihĕnta*

apa tan pasahāya tuṅga-tuṅgal,
phalamūlāśana yāmaṅan gĕgāṅan,
daluwaŋ wĕḍihanya rūkṣa duḥka,
ikanaŋ sakṣaṇa yālahāta dènta*

taya doṣa nya tuwi n pĕjaḥ ya dèṅku*

#pañcamas saṙggaḥ#
<rajanī>:5.1
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ : 17

atha ri pĕjaḥ nikaŋ triśira śīghra hulū nya tibā,
dadi ta masö masĕṅhit ikanaŋ khara dūṣaṇa lèn,
saha bala maṅlayaŋ kadi ta mégha katon ahirĕŋ,
karatala kadga cakra winawa nya-ya tulya kilat*

hana mamanaḥ wanèḥ kadi ta bajra panaḥ nya biṣa,
tali ni panaḥ nya rodra kumupak kaharan gĕlapa,
raghusuta bāyubajra ya paḍā ni panaḥ nira bāp,
ya ta kumĕnékanaŋ kala tibā sahana nya pĕjaḥ*

ri pati nikaŋ musuḥ si khara dūṣaṇa lèn triśiraḥ,
makin asekĕl gĕlāna ta si Śūṙppanakā manaṅis,
dadi malayū tĕkènajarakĕn ta kaka nya pĕjaḥ,
ri sira ta saŋ daśānana masö ya mahā manĕsĕl*

prabhu kita rāwaṇātiśaya śakti jayèŋ bhuwana,
praṇata musuḥta bhakti matakut sahana nya kabèḥ,
surapati saŋ hyaŋ indra tuwi bhakti sira praṇata,
katham api duṙnaya pwa kita hīna tamat panulus*

hana kari cārakanta ya kinon mahasèŋ prĕthiwī,
sumusupanāŋ alas biṣama śatru hanā matapa,
ya tika tahānta haywa humĕnĕŋ pwa kitèŋ biṣama,
ya Ika kaduṙṇnayanta Amĕṅāmni balanta pĕjaḥ*

si kara si dūṣaṇa triśira sūra sudhīra pĕjaḥ,
lumaku kinon matuṅgwa rikanaŋ giri Ḍaṇḍaka ya,
mati kapisan taman pabisa dé nika saŋ matapa,
prakaśita rāma lakṣmaṇa mati ya taman pamales*

sahana-hananta mātya kita dé nya si dāśarati,
ya ta walĕsĕnta toḥ kira-kiran pĕjaha nya huwus,
saphala Ikā kasĕṅhitakĕnéka pĕjaḥ nya kabèḥ,
apan anipis pagĕṙtta yadiyan mahurip biṣama*

kita mamaṅan magoṣṭi maṅinum saha bhrĕtya wijaḥ,
wiṣaya kasakta tat-t-aṅĕn-aṅĕn ŋ Awasāna pijer,
kita wĕgig iŋ musuḥ daṅu-daṅu magĕlöm aṅawit,
hana paribhūta śatru tamatan pamalĕs pwa mĕné*

rikanaŋ alas ri Ḍaṇḍaka siraŋ tapa taṙ matakut,
pratidina homayajña ginawé nira kapwa lanā,
tuwi taya rākṣasāṅipik-ipik rikanaŋ patapan,
raghusuta rāma lakṣmaṇa Ataḥ katakut nya kabèḥ*

rasika ta saŋ raghūttama taman pasahāya tuwi,
inatus-atus ta rowaŋ ikanaŋ khara dūṣaṇa bāp,
punaṙ api tan hanāmyati matap mati yāguliṅan,
ikana panaḥ niraŋ raghusutādbhuta mrĕtyu juga*

dadhi ghrĕta māṅsa matsya pinaṅan phala dibya raṣa,
surawara déwatā ya pinaṅan ya warĕg ya mĕné,
ikana balanta rākṣasa humöt ya kabèḥ malapā,
alaḥ atakut ri saŋ prawara rāghawa lakṣmaṇa ya*

ya tika dumèḥ kitāmriha mabuddhya-ya laṇḍĕpana,
wiṣaya-ya tāryakĕn maran agöŋ ta hayunta lanā,
atiśaya cañcalékanaŋ inak kṣaṇa matra hilaŋ,
ya ta kĕmitĕn prihĕnta gawayĕnta ŋ upāya huwus*

wwara ta ya ghāra saŋ raghusutottama riŋ rahayu,
awak akilākiris mrĕdu ya komala konĕŋ-unĕŋ,
swara nira haṅsanāda mamanis juga yan karĕṅö,
ya ta Alapĕnta liṅku saphalān kawawéri kita*

ataha-tahan matanta Apa tapwan anoṇ ḍahayu,
ikana Iruṅta tan saphala yan tan ikārĕkana,
tuwi taliṅanta niṙ-guṇa ya tan paṅujaṙ nya rĕṅön,
suka paripūṙṇna riŋ hayu Asiŋ kahanan rasikā*

sari-sari niŋ rasātiśaya sāri nikaŋ wiṣaya,
yan ika jugānakĕbya tat aṅipya wanèha ta ya,
asiŋ umulat riyāhyuna manaḥ nya sumomaha ya,
tribhuwanarājya yéka palaku nya wĕlīna ta ya*

hari-dayitā Śacī tuwi taman pamaḍāna hayu,
girisuta rohiṇī rati apūṙwwa taman pamaḍé,
hayu rasikā kabèḥ rahayu liŋ niŋ apuṅguŋ ikā,
anakĕbi saŋ raghūttama jugāhayu liṅku putus*

ya Ikana liŋ nikāŋ adhama Śūṙppanakān pawuwus,
ri sira ta saŋ daśānana wawaŋ sumahuṙ ta sira,
ari kita haywa cāla hrĕdayanta tamat t-alara,
takarin iké si rāwaṇa ṅaranya jayèŋ bhuwana*

syapa karikā tinonta kinabhaktyan iŋ indra kunĕŋ,
kuliśa ta śīṙṇna bajra ri ḍaḍaṅku taman paṅani,
hana ta liman hyaŋ indra sinikĕpku taman paṅapa,
ḍukut upama nya tan paguṇa dèṅku tinimpalakĕn*

nda taṅa-taṅā prabhāwa ni si rāwaṇa tan papaḍa,
satata mara ŋ wulan Umĕtu pūṙṇnama taṙ wiluma,
mamawa wuṅa n tahun sahana niŋ hyaŋ alaḥ matakut,
sa Isi nikaŋ surālaya Anéka kahĕnti kabèḥ*

ikana wuwusta hāsya mata kéraŋ-iraŋ dahatĕn,
yak atukarāpraṅa mwaŋ ikaṅaŋ tapa dāśarathī,
tuwi ya manūṣya hīnabala tan hana śakti riya,
saka riyasiḥku tag wihaŋ asiŋ sapakonta rari*

atha ri huwus nirominaki citta si Śūṙppaṇakā,
lumaku sirāhawan gagana śīghra manojawana,
pratita si candrahāsa ya tĕwĕk nira tan kapasaḥ,
satĕka nirèŋ samudra sumĕpĕṙ ta sirèŋ pasisi*

mara-marahaŋ marīca ya ta don ira yan sĕpĕra,
sateka nirāṙ waraḥ ta si marīca ri karya nira,
dadi sumahuṙ satorasi mataṅguḥ alaḥ matakut,
ya huwus alaḥ pwa ṅūni pinanaḥ riŋ aṅin ya katūb*

prabhu kita hé daśānana nanā kita yat malagā,
lawan ika saŋ raghuprawara rāma ya śakti tĕmĕn,
ikana si candrahāsa ya tĕwĕkta taman paṅapa,
mataŋ ika haywa māra Irikaŋ tapa dāśarathi*

hana sira jāmadagni wiku śakti matī ratu bāp,
saŋ umĕjahīkaŋ aṙjjuna sahasrabhujèŋ palagan,
syapa karĕṅö Anuŋ malahakĕn sira tan hana lèn,
raghusuta kéwalāta winuwus sira śakti jaya*

nya ta ya si tāṭakākya bali māti tĕkap rasikā,
atha ri sĕḍĕŋ mayajña sira saŋ rĕṣi kampalayu,
kapati gupuy ṅhulun kapalupuy pinanaḥ riŋ aṅin,
prabhu ta turuŋ tamad wruḥ i gĕlis nira yan pamanaḥ*

atiśaya riŋ dhanuṙddhara raghūttama taṙ papaḍa,
taku-takutĕn nikaŋ asura rākṣasa taṙ papuliḥ,
samĕna nikaŋ waṅal mati cĕṅĕl nya pĕgat pinanaḥ,
si khara si dūṣaṇa triśira śīṙṇna sudhīra pĕjaḥ*

umilu sirèŋ swayambara ri yajña niraŋ janaka,
hana ta laras Umuṅgu ri tĕṅaḥ nikanaŋ pasabhān,
sahana niraŋ ratu pwa ya mayat ya taman kawĕnaŋ,
katham api saŋ raghūttama mayat ya tikĕl wĕkasan*

kita suka kéwalāwĕrö-wĕrö mamaṅan maṅinum,
saha bala matta māṅsaka surā Ininumta lanā,
amija-mijaḥ sĕkaṙ jĕnu sugandha jĕnĕk riŋ inak,
ndya ta gamananta tat Alaha riŋ raṇa dé rasikā*

nahan ujaṙ iŋ marīca ya mataṅguḥ akon maluya,
muji guṇa saŋ raghūttama ri śakti nirātiśaya,
mĕdi-mĕdi saŋ daśānana ya donya Alaḥ matakut,
dadi magĕlĕŋ ta saŋ daśamukhāsi wawaŋ sumahur*

guragaḍa ko marīca hatinīca wimūḍa cĕmĕr,
ikana Ujaṙ-mu jañjan ujaṙ iŋ maṅajap juga ya,
umalahakĕn siraŋ paraśurāma sirékin alaḥ,
apan atuhā kĕlut sira si rāma sĕḍĕŋ taruṇa*

ikana si tāṭakā pinĕjahanya taman sapujin,
anakĕbi tan pasāra tuwi tan pasabāya ta ya,
ya ta pinanaḥ ni rāghawa ya niṙghrĕṇa tan paguṇa,
yadiyan ikā pujinta lalu hātmu yu dhik laku mūr*

tuwi pinanaḥ ni rāghawa ta ko Atikaṣṭa dahat,
wĕdi-wĕdi hīna nīca rumaras ta manahmu kawĕs,
ikana panaḥ nya manda taman ādrĕs aṅinya malon,
saka ri takutmu mamriḥ alayū juga tan Inapa*

hana ta Ujaṙmu lèn umuji śakti ni dāśarathi,
anikelakĕn laras Apan awūk malawas kinĕkĕs,
ya pinaṅan iŋ bubuk gilig-gilig ya dumèḥ nya nana,
ikaŋ umayat ya tambayan ataḥ lalu hīna dahat*

pati nikanaŋ kara triśira tan ya dumèḥ ya pujin,
apan akĕlé pramāda ya dumèḥ nya kabèḥ pĕjaha,
yan agalakāṅlagāna ri si rāghawa ghoratara,
niyata pĕjaḥ ni rāghawa rikaŋ kṣaṇa taṙ paṅapa*

ndya ta ya pujimwa śakti ni si rāghawa koŋ adhama,
druhaka jugāharĕp maliha buddhimu bhaktya riya,
mataŋ ika kompujīriya guṇaṅku tamaṙ puji ya,
jaga-jaga mātya ko druhaka cittamu taṇ ḍahayu*

atha ri huwus nirāṅuman-uman maṅunus ta tĕwĕk,
kumĕtĕṙ ikā kumis nira humīs hariṅĕt niŋ awak,
kadi tinĕpak kabāṅan ikanaŋ muka bhīṣaṇa ya,
tudiṅi tikaŋ marīca ya manĕmbaḥ aminta hurip*

Ṅhulun ikihĕn patik praṇata bhakti taman druhaka,
tuhu-tuhu bhakti riŋ prabhu Asiŋ sapakona riya,
ikana kunaŋ dumèḥ ṅhulun ataṅguha dhaṙmma tinūt,
prakrĕti nikanaŋ manéwaka mataṅguha donya hitā*

yadiyapi yat pituhwa hayu niŋ naya tan wihaṅĕn,
sarahayu sèṣṭi saŋ prabhu ya tūtĕna dadyakĕna,
nahan ikanaŋ Upāya yadiyan kĕna yat pituhun,
tĕmahana ni ṅhulun kidaŋ arambuta mās kanaka*

ikana si rāma lakṣmaṇa ya dohakĕnaṅkwa huwus,
ri wuri nikā sakèṣṭi nira nātha taman warahĕn,
nahan ujariŋ marīca wĕkasan maduluṙ lumaku,
tĕka ya rikāŋ alas matĕmahan ta kidaŋ kanaka*

marakatawaṙṇna rāmya makiris ta gigiṙ nya katon,
ikana wulu nyawak nya malĕṅis ya kabèḥ mas abāŋ,
tĕka ya masö ri saŋ janakarājasutā ya mariŋ,
kadi giniraŋ-giraŋ hati nirādbhuta dé nya jenĕk*

iniṅĕt-iṅĕt nirāhayu kulit nya kĕmul-kĕmula,
apan alĕṅis katon kanaka rambut alĕmbut alit,
hati nira tībra dé nira harĕp ri hayu nya katon,
dadi ta makon makoliha rikaŋ mrĕga ratnamaya*

raghusuta taṙ wihaŋ juga Asiŋ sapakon i sira,
ari nira lakṣmaṇa ta kawĕkas makĕmit patapan,
lumaku siromusī ya sinikĕp nira tan kawĕnaŋ,
apan agĕlis lumumpat analimpĕtakĕn mawilĕt*

kadi ya mariŋ mahā ya sakarĕŋ maṅadĕg maparö,
wahu tinalandaṅan ya sinikĕp nira śīghra mĕsat,
apan alĕyö wulu nya malĕṅis linĕṅan juga ya,
kamaga taṅan nirān kaluputan malayū ya muwaḥ*

dadi ta madoḥ uliḥ nira manūti taman kawĕnaŋ,
tuwi maṅidīdi yāmarimisin maṅadĕg sakarĕŋ,
hati nira héwa dé nya tamatan kawĕnaŋ sinikĕp,
r-ayat ikanaŋ laras r-araḥ-araḥ ya rikaŋ warayaŋ*

kadi hinarit higā nya mĕtu rāḥ nya Usus nya mulū,
wĕkasi hurip nya yékana pawū nya mamañcana ya,
janakasutā gĕlāna rumĕṅö ri taṅis nya mawās,
kadi ta ya śabda saŋ prawara rāma maminta tuluŋ*

dadi manaṅis siraŋ janakarājasutā ta mawū,
laku ta Ariṅku lakṣmaṇa tuluŋ pwa kakanta tasön,
kita marikénuhuḥ nira makon umarātuluṅa,
lalu tan asiḥta riŋ kaka tasö pwa tarākṣa sira*

ya Ikana liŋ niraŋ janakarājasutāṙ panaṅis,
saka ri y-asiḥ niréki panahā nikanaŋ hrĕdaya,
dadi sumahuṙ ta saŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇa tan kagĕmĕr,
pracaya ri śakti saŋ kaka rikaŋ raṇa taṙ malaha*

kita raghuwīraghāra kaḍasiḥ ni kakaṅku kita,
athawa naréndra saŋ janakarāja bapanta sira,
lalu ta ya dènta hīna kagĕmö rumĕṅö manaṅis,
sira karikānaṅis syapa wĕruḥta kunaŋ ya hadé*

syapa kari śakti riŋ bhuwana liṅta Anuŋ wĕnaṅa,
lumawana saŋ naréndrasuta rāghawa riŋ palagan,
sira juga śaktimānta wihikan ta riŋ astra kabèḥ,
ndya ta ya kasaṅśayān pĕjaha paṇḍuk ikaŋ hariṇa*

syapa wĕka saŋ raghūttama Anuŋ rinĕṅönta daṅū,
alaḥ atakut ya mātya mamalakwa ta rakwa tuluŋ,
sahana nikaŋ watĕk raghu kabèḥ tak anon alayū,
mati ya mamūk taman mawĕdi yan hana śatru biṣa*

athawa Ikaŋ kidaŋ kadi mahā maharĕp pĕjaha,
rasa ri y-ulaḥ nya kādbhuta tumon sira tan matakut,
atisaphalāstra saŋ raghusuta pwa ya donya pĕjaḥ,
maturun apuy hiḍĕp nya ri panaḥ nira bahnimaya*

syapa karikā tan ādbhuta tumon raghuputra haraḥ,
jaya rikanaŋ musuḥ sira taman papaḍĕŋ bhuwana,
mataŋ ika haywa śoka kita dé nikanaŋ manaṅis,
muliha kakanta rāghawa makoliḥ ikaŋ hariṇa*

ikanaŋ awū taman sira Ikā kala rākṣasa ya,
kira-kira bañcanékana ya don i Uni nya mahā,
taṅis ikanaŋ kidaŋ ikana liṅku huwus pinanaḥ,
umaḍa-maḍékanā swara niraŋ raghusiṅha juga*

atha ri huwus niraŋ taruṇa lakṣmaṇa yaṙ pawuwus,
janakasutā tataṙ pamituhu pwa Amogha wihaŋ,
ikanaŋ asiḥ takut ya maṅawéśa rikaŋ hrèdaya,
dadi sumahuṙ mrĕṣodita wuwus nira taṇ ḍahayu*

ari kita saŋ sumitratanayāpa kalīṅan ikā,
wahu-wahu dènta māmbĕk alĕmöḥ ri pakonku mĕné,
atiśaya bhakti riŋ daṅu-daṅū kita sātya kaka,
punaṙ api duṙbala pwa sira hīna tamat patuluŋ*

wruḥ aku ri don i buddhimu kaṭuṅka tamaṇ ḍahayu,
druhaka ri saŋ raghūttama manahmu harĕp wipatha,
atiśaya duṙjanādhama dahat raghuwaṅśa kariḥ,
wĕnaŋ abhimāna riŋ kaka Aḥ o Atikaśmala ya*

ikana Aṅĕn-aṅĕnmu ri siraŋ raghupūtra nihan,
mati sira dé nikaŋ mrĕga sadé nya sabhāgya tĕmĕn,
sumiliha tāku riŋ janakarājasutāku baśā,
syapa śaraṇā nya tan hana wanèḥ aku liṅmu nihan*

adhama wimūḍa lakṣmaṇa waliṅmu manaḥku kalā,
wĕnaṅa makāmbĕka ṅhala matāku mahalwana wèḥ,
aku tak aṅĕn-aṅĕn laki wanèḥ sira tuṅgal ataḥ,
makahulunāku tan hana wanèḥ raghuputra juga*

yan alalisāŋ bhaṭāra pĕjahāta siraŋ siniwi,
raghusuta sora riŋ samara paṇḍuk ikaŋ hariṇa,
pĕgatakĕnaṅkwa tékana guluṅkwa turūn apuya,
tumutura tāku riŋ priya tamāg wĕgilāta ri ko*

ya Ikana liŋ niraŋ janakarājasutā magĕlĕŋ,
maṅuman-uman Amogha wulaṅun maharĕp mahalā,
hala ni manaḥ nirāta juga tan tinahān mahalā,
saka ri wirodha niŋ hati mataŋ nya halān tinahā*

daśarathaputra lakṣmaṇa gĕlāna ta mépu sira,
atiśaya dibya tékana wuwus nira yan karĕṅö,
naya nira yukti tékana lalu pwa ya tan kahiḍĕp,
ya ta lumaré manaḥ nira wawaŋ sumahuṙ ta sira*

Ṅhulun ikihĕn sinaṅśaya kalā druhakāk makaka,
ikana manaḥku śuddha juga satya taman kalana,
sahana baṭāra sākṣya ni hatiṅku siromulata,
naraka tĕmuṅkwa duḥka hiḍĕpĕṅkwa yadin druhakā*

janakasutā samaṅkana kitāt mawuwus mahala,
kadi maṅajap sumaṅguḥ aku mahyuna wèḥ ri kita,
saka ri wuwusta taṇ ḍahayu duḥka tĕmunta magöŋ,
tawanĕn ikāŋ musuḥ kita mĕné ri wuriṅku haraḥ*

nahan ika liŋ nirāṙ panapathé dadi śīghra sira,
laku tumutūṙ i saŋ kaka tumūta manūta kidaŋ,
ri wuri niromadĕg janakarājasutā wĕkasan,
lumaku mamèt sĕkaṙ sira ri saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ patapan*

atha ri sĕḍĕŋ nirāmupu sĕkaṙ manusup riŋ alas,
tĕka ta siraŋ daśānana mahāṙddhika rūpa nira,
wiku śuci śuddha Śꜽwa sira sātwika śānta katon,
hulu malĕṅis ginuntiŋ aratā hana kuñciṙ alit*

atiśaya śuddha huntu maputiḥ sphaṭikopama ya,
tuwi magaṇitrikuṇḍala waluḥ ya sinaṇḍaŋ ira,
lituhayu waṙṇna lāka daluwaŋ nira rāmya mabāŋ,
lumaku manasya yéka dalihan Ira tan katĕṅĕr*

majapa maṅunyakĕn ta sira mantra tĕhĕṙ lumaku,
mrĕdu mamanis wulat nira marūm atisomya katon,
ikana karākṣasān ira kadi pwa ya tan hana wèḥ,
tama ta macaṅkramé tĕpi niŋ āśrama rāmya kabèḥ*

tinĕmu nirā ta saŋ janakarājasutā riŋ alas,
sira juga tuṅga-tuṅgal anusup tamataṙ matakut,
dadi ta masö siraŋ daśamukhātisahaṙṣa sira,
makin aparö sagorawa sirān pawuwus wĕkasan*

apa kita dibya rūpa manusup maṅalap ta sĕkar,
atiśaya tā paḍanta rikanaŋ hayu pūṙṇna tĕmĕn,
hayu nikanaŋ wulan tuwi taman pamaḍéri kita,
apan awĕnĕs ya riŋ rahina hīna tamaṙ pasĕnö*

kusuma saroja riŋ talaga kapwa sĕḍĕŋ sumĕkar,
rahayu sugandha waṙṇna ya mabaŋ maputiḥ sawanèḥ,
tuwi tamatan paḍékana hayu nya masoṙ juga ya,
apan umaluy kucup ya rikanaŋ wĕṅi taṇ ḍahayu*

iki kahananta bhīṣaṇa Amānuṣagamya sukĕt,
tan awĕdi riŋ ulā biṣama lèn aliman magalak,
syapa śaraṇānta liṅku yadiyan hana moŋ maṅawit,
ikana hayunta héman ari yogya kahātakĕna*

kita mrĕdu komalātiśaya konĕŋ-unĕŋ ri hati,
kadi ta bhinūsaṇan Ikaŋ alas ri hananta riya,
saṅapa ṅarān irāta sira saŋ siniwinta kunĕŋ,
atiśaya göŋ ni dhaṙmma rasikān pamawéri kita*

aku ta paribhramanta paradéśa rikaŋ bhuwana,
tuwi tak anon anuŋ paḍa-paḍānta surūpa tĕmĕn,
kita juga hīṅa niŋ hayu ya liṅku tanora wanèḥ,
saphala Iké huripku ri huwusku weruḥ ri kita*

ikana hayunta yāk iṅĕt-inĕt ya kadi pwa sĕkar,
huwus inisĕp nikaŋ bhramara téka sari nya rurū,
hana ta hayu nya mātra kawĕkas ya paḍanta katon,
ya ta panĕṅĕṙku Awas ya sira siniwīnta hana*

ikana bhaṭāra wiṣṇu tuwi marya sirāṙ pahiyun,
i sira ta saŋ priyā nira masoṙ sira dènta tĕmĕn,
athawa bhaṭāra kāma sira kāmuka liṅku pijĕr,
ri sira ta saŋ ratiḥ nira taman pamaḍéri kita*

sahana nikaŋ anakkĕbi tuwin yadiyan wulata,
niyata ya kādbhuté kita manaḥ nya kapūhan ataḥ,
ṅuni-ṅuni tékanaŋ taruṇa yan wruha mahyuna ya,
pira warĕga nya riŋ wiṣaya matta bhatāra tuwi*

hana ta daridra duḥkita tuwin mari yan pahiyun,
yan apa ya tāsihériya sumaṇḍiṅa yèŋ śayana,
maṅayam-ayam mahas mabayaṅan hati saŋ wiṣayī,
kita yatikāmrĕtosadha niraŋ kĕna kāmaśara*

wĕka-wĕka sāṅapéki sira saŋ siniwinta kunĕŋ,
lalu wihikan Irān hana kitèŋ patapān asukĕt,
saka ri takut nirān hana wanèha tumona kita,
yatika dumèḥ sirānusup umuṅgu rikaŋ patapan*

daśamuka nā ta liŋ nira sahaṙṣa sirāṙ pawuwus,
janakasutā sagadgada manaḥ nira yan pinuji,
hati rumaras puhun wulu niromuririŋ matakut,
praṇata sirāṙ paśabda mawaraḥ ta ri saŋ siniwi*

wwara sira rāma dāśarathi śakti tamaṙ papaḍé,
sira rasiké Anuŋ makahulun ṅhulun āṙyyaguṇa,
atiśaya bhakti riŋ bapa siromituhu ŋ sapakon,
sahana niraŋ tapaswi sira rākṣaka riŋ patapan*

sahana nikā musuḥ nira mahāṙṣi pinatyan ira,
sira ta sumorakĕn paraśu rāma rikaŋ palagan,
sira kumĕmit mahāṙṣi yan ahoma mayajña lanā,
mara ta sirèŋ alas saka ri bhakti nirāṙ mabapa*

Śatèka nirèŋ alas hana ta rākṣasa sāhasika,
ya ta lumagé sirāṙ teka parĕŋ maṅabèhi masö,
saha bala śaktimānta sahana nya pĕjaḥ pinanaḥ,
ri tĕpi niŋ āśramāt taṅa-taṅā hana waṅkay atap*

sira karĕṅö dhanuṙddhara rikaŋ bhuwanāṇḍa kabèḥ,
magada-gadāna dadya tamatan hana koli nira,
kadi pinusus tikaŋ musuḥ asiŋ umasö kapisan,
kita kadi molya mĕṅgĕp amĕpöri siraŋ siniwi*

ikana mataŋ nya tan katĕmu dènta nihan ya rĕṅön,
wwara ya kidaŋ hĕmas ya Inusi nira kādbhuta ya,
ari nira lakṣmaṇéka kawĕkas wĕkasan tumutur,
saka ri pakonku yékana dumèḥ nira taṙ wihaṅa*

atha ri huwus niraŋ janakarājasutāṙ pawaraḥ,
makin umasö siraŋ daśamukāṙ pawuwus ta muwaḥ,
wruḥ aku rikā si rāghawa ṅaranya taman paguṇa,
apa ta dumèḥ kitāhyun iriyā ri kaniṣṭa dahat*

adhama masoṙ ya saṅka ri Ari nya kabèḥ wihikan,
ya matuha yogya ratwa ya kinon pwa marékiŋ alas,
mamati-matīka rākṣasa Asiŋ mara riŋ patapan,
ndya ta ya kawismayanta ri si rāghawa hīnaguṇa*

ndak ajaṙ-ajaṙ kitāri Ikanaŋ ratu śakti tĕmĕn,
hana ri parākrama nya ya dumèḥ nya manĕmwa suka,
sahana nikaŋ jagattraya taman hana moli riya,
ya ta Ikahĕn si rāwaṇa ṅaranya yatéki ḍatĕŋ*

aku ta jayèŋ surālaya manuṣya carācara lèn,
ikana bhaṭāra wꜽśrawaṇa sāmpun alaḥ sinukū,
yama ya maminta jīwita Alaḥ matakut pĕjaha,
surapati saŋ hyaŋ indra ya ta bhakti kabèḥ praṇata*

kadi ta karĕm rikaŋ tasik ikaŋ suraloka kabèḥ,
paḍa mawĕnĕs kagöman asamun sahana nya maruk,
hana nikanaŋ prabhāwa ni si rāwaṇa tulya riwut,
ya ta katakut nikaŋ sura dumèḥ nya masoṙ arusak#

#saṭ saṙggaḥ#
<waṅśastha>:6.1
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ : 12

ikā kaḍatwanku samīpa niŋ tasik,
gahan ri lĕṅkā kadi kānti niŋ wulan,
i ratnapārāyaṇa nāma tan kalèn,
ri dé nyan akwèḥ maṇiratna yojwala*

ya tékanānuŋ kawaśākĕnanta ya,
mamuktya lāwan n-aku haywa saṅśaya,
asiŋ sakahyunta hana ta yériya,
kawīt ta kĕmbaŋ haḍaṅĕn saménaka*

sayogya sampat Ika liṅku kāsiha,
ṅhulun sĕḍĕŋ yowana śaktimānta ya,
awakta saśrī yuwatī sĕḍĕŋ hayu,
si rāma tātaṙ paguṇāri tāryakĕn*

paṅan Inum saṅgama yéka bhuktinĕn,
ṅhulun-hulun tulya manĕmbahé kita,
tadĕg ri lĕṅkā nda huwus ta liṅkwari,
awakta yékā hyasi wèhĕn adyana*

ujaṙ niraŋ rāwaṇa yaṙ panomaha,
sitā tan aṅgā humĕnĕŋ taman sahur
daśāsya sakrodha masö sirāṅgyakĕn,
sitā pinuṇḍut nira śīghra maṅlayaŋ*

gĕlāna dèwī janakātmajānaṅis,
masū masāmbat karĕṅö rikaŋ laṅit,
kidaŋ manuk riŋ patapan paḍomĕnéŋ,
kagömanānon riŋ ulaḥ samaṅkana*

Ꜽ rāma hé rāghawa niṙghrĕṇanta wèḥ,
lukan kĕtékā tan asiḥta ri ṅhulun,
asiŋ pakon taṙ dadi laṅghanā Ataḥ,
waliṅku siḥ té ry aku haḥ lalis kariḥ*

lanā marīntoṣa kitāṅiriŋ manaḥ,
widagda riŋ citta mariŋ anakkĕbi,
asiŋ sakahyunku dinadyakĕnta ya,
ṅhulun-n-atékīnuguṅan kināsihan*

samaṅkanāriṅku si lakṣmaṇottama,
aḥ-o mahāprajña rikaŋ nayèṅgita,
ujaṙ jugākās kadi śabda niŋ wihaŋ,
hatinta māsiḥ takarin tĕmĕn-tĕmĕn*

kṣamākĕna ujaṙkkwi kitāri lakṣmaṇa,
ayogya tātan parĕṅönta yāhala,
swabhāwa niŋ strī juga niṙwiwéka ya,
kalotakĕn haywa kitāgĕlĕŋ ry aku*

kakanta saŋ rāma lukan lalis nira,
parintuṣāsiḥ sapakonku taṙ wihaŋ,
kitāt wihaŋ ṅūni sakèŋ asiḥ kariḥ,
ṅhulun Ataḥ pātaka nīca kaśmala*

piré kadhīrān ira saŋ mahāṙddhika,
rĕṅö wuwus niŋ kala mūṙ ataḥ sira,
mataŋ nya yuktīka ta dènta taṙ salaḥ,
saké kaḍuṣṭan ni wuwusku mūṙ kita*

ikāpi saŋ sajjana yan winèḥ ujar,
gĕlĕŋ nirèŋ wwaŋ sapĕtik tamaṙ lanā,
tinon irékaŋ kala duḥka kāsyasiḥ,
amogha māsiḥ umasö sirānuluŋ*

mataŋ nya hé lakṣmaṇa sādhu sajjana,
tasö tuluṅtāku gĕlāna duḥkita,
ikā wuwustānapathé lukan tuhu,
nihan ṅhulun wèḥ tinawan-n-ikaŋ musuḥ*

nahan pasāmbat janakātmajāṙ pawū,
humuŋ sirāminta tuluŋ masāmbatan,
jaṭāyu kāwit sira mārĕṅö taṅis,
mĕsat siraṙ ton sira saŋ daśānana*

daśānanātyanta rikaŋ kalādhama,
musuḥ niraŋ tāpasa mūṙkka sāhasa,
wĕnaŋ masampay paribhūta riŋ wiku,
tasö huwus yan tuhu wīra riŋ raṇa*

ikāpi saŋ rāghawa mmāsiḥ iŋ wiku,
ya sātwikāsiḥ tuwi bhakti riŋ bapa,
wĕnaŋ pwa ko sāhasa dhik kalādhama,
lukan tan éraŋ lumarèŋ mahāṙddhika*

jaṭāyu yéki ta bhaṭāra bhāskara,
umatyanaŋ mūṙkka kabèḥ tamomaya,
patik-patik saŋ raguputra tékihĕn,
rĕṇāku ṅūnin pakamitra saŋ bapa*

<Śāṙddūlawikrīḍta>:6.19
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ : 19

nāhan liŋ nira saŋ jaṭāyu Umasö masyaŋ Umuŋ syāpraṅa,
kumlab téka hĕlaṙ nirādbhuta makas malwā malaṇḍĕp kabĕḥ,
śāṙddūlākrĕti siṅhatulya magalak śīghrāmarĕk sāhasa,
tuṇḍāghāta patuk nirāyudha nirālaṇḍĕp ya bajropama*

yékān sāhasa saŋ daśānana r-unus taŋ candrahāsākilat,
haṙṣāmbĕk nira saŋ jaṭāyu maṅĕpö rodran panampyal muka,
munduṙ yatna siromilag Inayatan riŋ candrahāsomĕsat,
Āścaṙyyèkana saŋ daśānana mulat tĕṅhā jaṭāywī ruhur*

umyus téka hĕlaṙ nirāṙ papagakĕn saŋ rāwaṇāṙ tuṅkuli,
sakrodhāṙ pamatuk-patuk nya kapĕtĕk māṙ bāhu saŋ rāwaṇa,
muñcaṙ taŋ rudirāṙ isĕp ta ya muwaḥ munduṙ mĕsat riŋ laṅit,
maṅkin daṙppa sirāwĕrö minum ikā rāḥ-rāḥ niraŋ rāwaṇa*

képwan saŋ daśawaktra soṙ sira sukĕṙ suṅgwī siraŋ mꜽthilī,
sambé taŋ bala rākṣasāṅhabĕt ikaŋ aśwomibĕṙ taŋ ratha,
yĕkoṅgwan-n-ira maṅlayaŋ kuda manogāmi masö maṅdĕmak,
śīṙṇnāsāk rinĕmĕk rĕmuk kinĕpĕkan rĕmpak tibā taŋ ratha*

saŋ sītā sira muṅgu riŋ ratha tibā umrĕm sawèt niŋ takut,
mūṙccā riŋ gaganāntarāla maṅĕliḥ mosaḥ gĕlānomĕhaḥ,
miṅsoṙ śīghra siraŋ jaṭāyu sumuyug sāmbut ta saŋ mꜽthilī,
mahyā taŋ daśadéśadéwata humuŋ kapwādbhutāṅastuti*

pahyā niŋ surasaṅghadéwata lawan gandhaṙwwa kapwāmuji,
héwa krodha siraŋ daśānana nanā maṅkĕp tikaŋ bāhu mār,
lāwan rāḥ nya nirantaromĕtu humīs ndā tan hiḍĕp yālara,
maṅsö sāhasikāṅusī mabayaṅan méraŋ jaṭaywaṙ layū*

saŋ sītā pinĕkul nirāṙddha kapati glānāsi mosaḥ sira,
tan mādrĕs ta Ibĕṙ nirāṙddha malimĕṙ mamriḥ alaḥ kabwatan,
yan taṙ sāmbuta saŋ naréndratanayā byaktān pĕjaḥ yan tibā,
yékā hétu niraŋ jaṭāyu malimĕṙ tébĕṙ nirāṅkin malon*

mĕḥ prāptā ta siraŋ daśānana maṅèl maṅliḥ jaṭāyūmĕhāḥ,
mosaḥ mosyan asiŋ paran Ira tinūt dé saŋ daśāsyèŋ laṅit,
tan dwān tandaṅi saŋ jaṭāyu dumilaḥ taŋ candrahāsākilat,
sĕmpal taŋ lahuyaŋ huyuŋ nira tibān pinraŋ niraŋ rāwaṇa*

{puṣpitāgra}:6.27
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏓ : 12
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏓ : 13

daśawadana wawaŋ siromĕkul saŋ,
janakasutāṙ wiparīta tībra mūṙccā,
hana ta ratha wanĕḥ masö manuṅsuŋ,
pinakahawan Ira yaṙ uliḥ ri lĕṅkā*

{mālinī}:6.28
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ : 15

satĕka nira ri lĕṅkā glāna kāmāturāhyun,
hana ri hati nirāṅhiŋ mꜽthilī ūṣadhātaḥ,
winaliŋ ira Umaṅgā jānakī rājaputrī,
dadi ta sira Umaṅsö wèt nikaŋ rāga tībra*

sahana-hana nikaŋ wwil wīra yékā kinonkon,
umiṅĕtakĕna saŋ śrī rāmabhadrāṙ makiṅkiŋ,
alaḥ awĕdi ri dé nyan śīṙṇna taŋ rākṣasākwĕḥ,
daśawadana sirādwāhĕnti wadwā nirākraḥ*

ri laku nikana taŋ wwil cāra yāmratyawékṣa,
dadi ta sira sumomaḥ jānakī ndā tan aṅga,
tinudiṅan i kiwān lèn taṙ winĕḥ śabda ménak,
daśamuka sira mūṙkkātyanta maṅsö tan éraŋ*

pratidina sira mojaṙ ndan mahāsatya dèwi,
raghutanaya cinitta dé nikaŋ citta tan lèn,
salahasa sira mosaḥ saŋ daśāsyāsi maswī,
r-ujari bala nirāṙ kon jānakī rākṣa-rākṣan*

atha ri hana niraŋ śrī jānakī ṅkā ri lĕṅkā,
raghutanaya sirékātyanta saṇḍéha Āśa,
marahakĕna hilaŋ saŋ jānakī duṙnimitta,
manuk umuni masambat lwiṙ nya maṅsö manuṅsuŋ*

daśarathasuta tībra glāna maṅliḥ makiṅkiŋ,
janakatanaya haḥ āḥ bhāgya tékin katĕmwa,
mati pinaṅan ikaŋ moŋ mwaŋ tibā riŋ juraŋ lwaḥ,
capala ta kunaŋ oṅsil haḥ lukan kāsyasiḥ nya*

sĕḍĕŋ aṅaṅĕn-aṅĕn saŋ rāghawa bhrāntacitta,
tĕka ta sira saŋ antĕn ndān ikaŋ wéṣa rūkṣa,
makin alara sirāṙ ton wéṣa saŋ lakṣmaṇoruk,
niyata pati nikā saŋ mꜽthilī liŋ nirāśā*

dadi ta sira matakwan śīghra mojaṙ saŋ antĕn,
duga-duga sira mājaṙ satya bhaktīŋ kakāsiḥ,
raghutanaya gĕlānān paṅrĕṅö wrĕtamātra,
hati nira ya ta śiṙṇnān śūnya taŋ rāt hiḍĕp nya*

kadi ta hilaŋ umĕtwaŋ jīwa saṅké śarīra,
mamana-mana sirāṅhèl dé ni kiṅkiŋ nirākwèḥ,
alaḥ umaṅĕn-aṅĕn saŋ jānakī citta luṅhā,
satata ri pipi yan hīs luḥ nirādrĕs tan ampĕt*

ari janakasutā ndī déśa Uṅgwanta tājar,
sahuri Aku gĕlānāsyaŋ-syaŋ aswī masāmbat,
pijéṙ amupu sĕkaṙ kwèḥ nā mataŋ nyāt tan aṅsö,
athawa milu maṅajyaṅrĕṅwakĕn dhaṙmmaśāstra*

syapa ta kunaŋ ikānuŋ takwanaṅkwé wĕkasta,
wruha ta ri Amĕṅantānuŋ satorasya mojar,
bapa ta taṅisanaṅkwébuṅku yādoḥ taman wruḥ,
suragaṇa humĕnĕŋ dhik déwatā tan hanojar*

atiśaya Aku yatnāmèt kitèŋ déśa mamriḥ,
mara haku ri paturw-antèŋ daṅū tat kapaṅguḥ,
hana watu maratālwa ṅkāk paromèt kitātaḥ,
sahana ni hawalantāku k-parāmèt kitāntĕn*

masuk aku riŋ alas göŋ lèn pamètanta kĕmbaŋ,
katĕmu kusuma lumrā kīṙṇna laywan rurū kwèḥ,
saka ri panas ikaŋ wé kapwa lūm yātirūkṣa,
kadi saka ri lara nyān tat hanākūŋ ya māśā*

kusuma saphala dibyāsiḥ nya tībré kitāntĕn,
atiśaya kari kiṅkiŋ nyāṙ kasaḥ dènta monĕŋ,
aku kalana ta kāsiḥ puṣpa tātan paḍé ya,
taya kita tuwi dèwī tan pĕjaḥ dé nyunĕṅku*

apa kita mamarīkṣā donta mĕṅgĕp Umiṅgat,
prahasana ta kunaŋ don iŋ humöt guywa-guywan,
wĕtu ta rari huwus hé tan wruḥ iŋ śoka monĕŋ,
biṣama tiki huripkun tūta miṅgat pwa dènta*

aku muliḥ umatīkaŋ rākṣasa krūrakaṙmma,
apa kita tat anuṅsuŋ kolakĕntāku dèwī,
aparan ikana dosaṅkwī kitaŋ toḥ pwa tājar,
lalu kita lumaré ṅwaŋ bhakti māsiḥ pwa nitya*

giri gahana gunuŋ ndin takwanaṅkwé wĕkasta,
lalu talib i gĕlĕṅtāmogha héwāntat aṅliŋ,
hilaŋ ikana kadhīrankwāpasaḥ sakya dènta,
kadi dinudutakĕn mĕḥ mĕtwa jīwaṅku luṅhā*

aku manaṅis aböḥ mèḥ mĕtwa rāḥ niŋ matābaŋ,
satata Aku masāmbat tan katoliḥ pwa dènta,
yan ahuwusan kasihtāri mari-āku monĕŋ,
kita tamat awaraḥ riŋ karya luṅhā tat amwīt*

tuwi Ikana Arintā lakṣmaṇékāna tan wruḥ,
wruha rikana gĕlĕṅtātyanta sūkṣma nya mèwĕḥ,
hana kari magĕlĕŋ riŋ swāmi tātaṙ padoṣa,
atiśaya kita sadhwācāra śīlanta liṅku*

umara Aku maniñjo ṅkā ri pahyas-hyasanta,
hana ta ya wulakan lèn pañcuran ṅkākwaniñjo,
katĕmu ta pasiwontékīŋ daṅū ṅkā tamolaḥ,
aku malara kapūhan dé nya tan ton hana ṅkā*

nahan ikana taṅis saŋ rāmabadhrātimūṙccā,
kapati kadi tinunwan dé nikaŋ śokabahni,
pawana sumiriṙ alwan tis nya tātan ya tamba,
biṣa miṣani ya maṅdé mohita ṅwaŋ ta dé nya*

krama mawuṅu sirāṅliḥ péṙ ikaŋ luḥ ya madrĕs,
lumaku ta sira madyus tuṅga-tuṅgal sirākūŋ,
alara tuwi makiṅkiŋ tan hilaŋ déwa pūjā,
prakrĕti juga pajātyan saŋ mahāsatwa satya*

tĕlas ajapa mamūjāṅaṙccanèŋ hyaŋ masandhyā,
laku ta muwaḥ umèt saŋ jānakī riŋ alas göŋ,
katĕmu ta palagan saŋ rāwaṇa mwaŋ jaṭāyu,
hati nira sawitaṙkkān ton ikaŋ cihna niŋ praŋ*

ari taruṇa sumitrāsūta taṅsö ya tonton,
ahalĕpan iki mapraŋ rākṣasa ṅké ta ṅūni,
rudhira ya tumibābāŋ bāhu sĕmpal katimpal,
kawaca ratha nihan taŋ tuṅgaṅan kapwa śīṙṇna*

ndak iṅĕt-iṅĕt ikāntĕn yan mapékā ya mapraŋ,
susupi Ikanaŋ ālas mèt ikaŋ rākṣasa ṅké,
maluya Ika laraṅkun ton ikaŋ rāḥ ya lumra,
alĕmĕḥ aku humèt saŋ jānakī liŋ nirāśā*

manuk apa kunĕŋ apraŋ hāḥ lukan kadbhuta nya,
lahuyaŋ atiśayèŋ göŋ cihna nāhan katimpal,
apa pinarĕbutanyān tan patrĕṣṇèŋ hurip nya,
harĕpa kunĕŋ ikā saŋ jānakī donya tan lèn*

nahan ikana wuwus saŋ rāmabhadhrān paṅūha,
jwalita kadi tinunwan twas nira krodha muntab,
mata nira ya kabāṅan wĕtwakĕn taŋ kadhīran,
tribhuwana kadi śīṙṇnā dé nirālaḥ saroṣa*

kadi ta sira bhaṭāra aditya maṅkin satéja,
makin apupul atambĕḥ wikramotsāha wrĕddhi,
awak apanas ahosaḥ dé nikaŋ krodhabahni,
raghusuta kadi siṅhāsiṅhanādātidaṙppa*

syapa ta kunaŋ ikānaŋ wwil wĕnaŋ sāhasa ṅké,
rumabhasa sira saŋ śrī jānakī rājaputrī,
apa kariki si rāmāwĕdya riŋ śatru śakti,
mataŋ ika Awamānātyanta nīca nya duṣṭa*

dinakara tuwi soṙ hyaŋ sūṙyya dèhkwi prabhāwa,
giriwaraśata śīṙṇna sāgarāsāta dèṅku,
sahana-hana nikaŋ rāt hĕntya tātan paśéṣa,
uragapati Ulāgöŋ ṅkā ri pātāla śīṙṇnā*

nuni-ṅuni Ikanaŋ wwil hĕntya tātan paśéṣa,
dhanapati tuwi duḥkā yakṣa ya syūha mātya,
aku ta maliha kālomatyanaŋ kālamrĕtyu,
sakala bhuwana cūṙṇnā bhūmi dĕṅkun pusus ya*

surawara Awarāṅkwī ŋ indra mandālpaśakti,
gaganatala tan alwā dèṅku wèhĕṅkwahöta,
maluya laya Ikaŋ rāt rātri tulya nya śūnya,
asiŋ-asiṅa ta sādhyān dadya tan dadya madwā*

nahan ikana wuwus saŋ rāghawāsiṅhanāda,
tihaṅakĕn ikanaŋ hrū héwa sakrodha riŋ rāt,
prarudita manaṅis saŋ lakṣmaṇāsiḥ manĕmbaḥ,
muhutakĕn ikanaŋ rāt mātya tātan padoṣa*

raghusuta kita mithyātyanta momo wimoha,
wipatha ta ya katrĕṣṇantèŋ jagad gadgadāku,
apa kita kadi médan tan padon dènta māmbĕk,
ṅhulun alara gĕlānān ton kitātaḥ salaḥ ton*

gĕlĕŋ i hati ya tībrātyanta kāmāturāhyun,
wwaŋ apa wihikana ŋ waŋ manda maṅdāni citta,
takarin atiśayāglis buddhi médan pramāda,
dhrĕti ya ta dulura nyān ruddha taŋ rodrabahni*

apa ta guṇagaṇā niŋ krodha yan tūtananta,
ya mataŋ amuharopĕk duṙyyaśèŋ rāt ya pāpa,
kalawan ikana taŋ rāt tan hanātaḥ sadoṣa,
kita juga wiparīta glāna dé niŋ larāgöŋ*

{śloka}:6.64

nāhan taṅguḥ nirāŋ antĕn,
tuṣṭodhāni siraŋ kaka,
kapwānusup sirèŋ ālas,
adoḥ saṅka riŋ āśrama*

tatkālān panusup kāliḥ,
n-ton jaṭāyu manuk magöŋ,
tan byakta téka dé niŋ doḥ,
katon kadi gunuŋ magöŋ*

yéki mātī siraŋ sītā,
liŋ niraŋ rāma niścaya,
r-aṅsö tandaṅi taŋ pakṣi,
jaṭāyu mawuwus wawaŋ*

hé rāma hé raghusuta,
haywa sāhasa ri ṅhulun,
jaṭāyu tāku tan kālèn,
wruḥ tākun jānakīn pinèt*

nā liŋ niraŋ mahāpakṣi,
manĕmbaḥ saŋ raghūttama,
siraŋ jaṭāyu kāruṇya,
mitra kāsiḥ niraŋ bapa*

sira glāna kanin tībra,
tathāpi mahurip sira,
alaḥ humèṙ siraŋ rāma,
saṅka ri drĕḍha niŋ asiḥ*

tĕka pwa sira saŋ rāma,
mājaṙ ta sira riŋ musuḥ,
huwus mājaṙ pĕjaḥ sira,
sawèt niŋ tībra niŋ kanin*

sapĕjaḥ nira mūṙccāśā,
saŋ rāma manaṅis sira,
hé jaṭāyu mahādibya,
wĕnaŋ dhāraka riŋ hurip*

Śaṅka ry asiḥta mamitra,
bapaṅku kalulut tĕmĕn,
tumuluy tĕka riŋ putra,
aḥ-o dibyanta hé kaga*

sĕḍĕṅtāt mahurip ṅūni,
bapaṅku mahurip hiḍĕp,
ri pĕjaḥta kunĕŋ maṅké,
mĕnyāk uwuḥ-uwuḥ tĕmĕn*

huwus saŋ rāma manaṅis,
tunu waṅkay ikaŋ manuk,
maśoca ta mawèḥ piṇḍa,
muwaḥ luṅhā sirānusup*

hana rākṣasa kāścaṙyya,
bāhu nya madawī tĕmĕn,
malapā maharĕp māṅsā,
ya pinaṅguḥ nirèŋ alas*

musuḥ niŋ satwa yèḥ daṅū,
dīṙgghabāhu ṅaran ikā,
ya ta maṅsö sira krūra,
r-unus taŋ kadga tīkṣṇa ya*

sāṅsö nya rodra yāgalak,
pinraŋ nira taṅanya-ya,
sāmpun pĕgat pwa bāhu nya,
tibā ta yérikaŋ lĕmaḥ*

maluy ta ya ri jāti nya,
déwatārūpa yan katon,
lumrā téja nikāwak nya,
kadi saŋ hyaŋ diwākara*

maprĕśna ya ri saŋ rāma,
mamĕpöṙ i ṅaran ira,
lāwan don iŋ masusupan,
ya tinakwanakĕn ikā*

satorasi siraŋ rāma,
mawaraḥ ri ṅaran-n-ira,
lawan don iŋ masusupan,
sumiliḥ ta sirātakon*

apa jātinta hé sādhu,
kita déwakrĕtin katon,
nihan ta-pajara wanèḥ,
yan kasiddhā sadon mami*

yan kapaṅguha saŋ sitā,
lawan yan alaha ŋ musuḥ,
nahan takwan iraŋ rāma,
dadi mājaṙ-ajaṙ ta ya*

Ṅhulun ānak bhaṭārī Śrī,
ndan durācāra ta ṅhulun,
sĕḍĕŋ kwacaṅkramèŋ swaṙgga,
aṅlaṅkahi mahāmuni*

saṅké gĕlĕŋ niré ṅhulun,
manīmpa dadya rākṣasa,
kitātaḥ antaśāpāṅkwa,
apan putrāku dènta wèḥ*

kunaŋ donta kasiddhā ya,
saŋ dèwīnta kapaṅguha,
tinawan saŋ daśamuka,
ri lĕṅkā kahanan nira*

nihan gunuŋ parananta,
rĕṣyamūka ṅaran nikā,
hana ta wré tĕmu ṅkāna,
saŋ sugriwa ṅaran nira*

mahāṙddhika mahāśakti,
ndan glāna ta ya duḥkita,
ya tékānugrahānanta,
kaka nya ya ta patyani*

saŋ sugrīwa gĕlānonĕŋ,
ri saŋ tārā priyā nira,
inalap dé ni saŋ bāli,
bāli atyanta duṣṭa ya*

saŋ sugrīwa sĕḍĕŋ monĕŋ,
kadi lĕmbu lanaŋ sira,
tan winèḥ maswa rikanaŋ,
lĕmbu mānak wahū mĕtu*

mataŋ nya hé raghūputra,
paḍa duḥkanta yak hiḍĕp,
yan mitrā ŋ kapi sugrīwa,
sahāyāntāt patī musuḥ*

iké wuwusku tan madwā,
satyawākya ṅhulun tĕmĕn,
mitrānta ŋ kapi sugrīwa,
niyatālaḥ ni rāwaṇa*

sĕḍĕṅtāt masihériya,
awās ya bhaktya rī kita,
kita gurwa Ikā śisyā,
kāṙyyanta towi dadya-ya*

pira doha ni kāṙyyanta,
katĕmu ta ya dé nikā,
tuwi makwèḥ ta wadwā nya,
wré magöŋ śaktimānta ya*

mataŋ nya mitrā sugrīwa,
duḥka nya ya hilaṅakĕn,
marapwan pamalss dlāha,
kitātĕmwa lawan priyā*

nahan-n-ujaṙ nikaŋ déwa,
ikaŋ rākṣasa pūṙwwaka,
mĕsat ta yomibĕṙ luṅhā,
saŋ rāma manusup muwaḥ*

tinon irāŋ alas rāmya,
wwa-wwahan tamalaḥ matöb,
hilaŋ lapā nirānton ya,
tĕmu taŋ lwaḥ magöŋ suci*

madrĕs hilī nya mahĕniŋ,
umĕntas ta sirādulur,
tĕmu ŋ alas rāmya tĕmĕn,
manon ta sira tāpasī*

Śawarī téka jāti nya,
kulit kayu tapiḥ nikā,
waṙṇna nyawak nya mahirĕŋ,
kadi waṙṇna niŋ añjana*

rūpa nya sādhu tañcāla,
pragrĕhyapāda tulya ya,
wītarāga ya dhaṙmmèṣṭha,
phalāhāra lanā bratī*

sawulat nira saŋ rāma,
hilaŋ tékāna ṅhèl nira,
kadibyan iŋ brata magöŋ,
mojaṙ ta sira kādbhuta*

hé tāpasī mahāsādhu,
lalu dibyanta mabrata,
aparan lwiṙ ni pūjānta,
yat satyèŋ īśwarāṙccaṇa*

pitrĕpūjā kunaŋ nitya,
lanāsandhyā kunaŋ kita,
yat satya riŋ waca-wacan,
lawan carita saŋ wiku*

prastāwa niŋ tapa magöŋ,
kāma moha kunaŋ hilaŋ,
dhīra-bratātwaŋ aguru,
nā prakāra nikaŋ tapa*

nā liŋ saŋ rāma maprĕṣṇa,
irikaŋ śawarī bratī,
sādarojaṙ ta ya mawèḥ,
madhupaṙkka lawan phala*

om sājña hé kitaŋ rāma,
ṅhulun ta magawé tapa,
asiŋ sakawĕnaŋ dèṅku,
kasatyanku hĕlĕm-hĕlĕm*

kunaŋ hétuṅku mabrata,
maṅhanākĕn kasambégan,
utpatti bhaṭāra wiṣṇu,
luṅhā mara ri pātāla*

kĕna śāpa dé hyaŋ rudra,
ri kāla niŋ liṅgodbhāwa,
madātĕmahan warāha,
makastrī dèwī pātāla*

mijil pwa sira hyaŋ wiṣṇu,
makarūpa ta warāha,
umĕgil irikaŋ gunuŋ,
amaṅan hāraka mami*

tĕlas nya maṅkanomati,
śawa nya tinaḍaḥ mami,
ya tikāṅdadyakĕn duḥka,
awak mami nīla waṙṇna*

tāsyasiḥ hé kitaŋ rāma,
tusapi muka ni ṅhulun,
pūṙṇnā kitāntaśāpāṅkwa,
tāryakĕn kléśa ni ṅhulun*

nā liŋ saŋ śawarī bratī,
inusap dé niraŋ rāma,
paripūṙṇna siraŋ yogī,
gumanti maṅanugrahé*

hé saŋ rāma mahādibya,
wiṣṇu sakala yaṙ katon,
wĕnaŋ umalapi kléśa,
mataŋ nya malĕsa ṅhulun*

wānaradhipa sugrīwa,
ya mitrānta mahāṙddhika,
katĕmwa jānakī dénta,
nā liŋ nya dadi mokṣa ya*

{turagagati}:6.114

rāma lakṣmaṇa muwaḥ sira manusup,
riŋ-ŋ-alas pratita kampa ya karĕṅö,
kwèḥ kĕnas riya wisāta ya kasukan,
mwaŋ mahāmuni hanèŋ alas anusup*

trĕpti saŋ raghusutāṙ wulat iŋ alas,
rāmya kapwa manĕḍĕŋ kusuma matap,
n-ton ikaŋ talaga dibya ya manulus,
padma yéka maputiḥ tamalaḥ-alaḥ*

Śokacitta sira dé nya ta maṅaraŋ,
mꜽthilī sira lanā Inaṅĕn-aṅĕn,
wĕt nyunĕŋ nira kunaŋ dadi manaṅis,
glāna yaṙ wara-waraḥ ta Ari nira*

lakṣmaṇāri wulati ŋ talaga maho,
bhūṣaṇa nya Uni niŋ bhramara humuŋ,
kokilomuni malon ya salaki-bi,
hāḥ mahā juga ya mèdi riŋ apasaḥ*

padma rāmya sumĕkaṙ paḍa manĕḍĕŋ,
wintaŋ iŋ gagana soṙ ta hayu nikā,
komala nya ya mawèḥ lara ri hati,
śoka saŋ priyawiyoga mulati ya*

saŋ sĕḍĕŋ priyasamāgama kasukan,
dé nikaŋ bhramara haṅsa paḍa munī,
rāmanīya-ya manohara ya mrĕdu,
kaṙṇnaśūla ya ri saŋ priyawiraha*

kīṙṇna taŋ kusuma nitya ya marurū,
dé nikaŋ manuk i pādapa masiwo,
wwaŋ wimūḍa ta kunaŋ taman alara,
mwaŋ ri saŋ tan aharĕp suka wirati*

gandha niŋ sĕkaṙ arūm mara riŋ iruŋ,
mwaŋ manuk nya lumaré taliṅa muni,
rūpa niŋ kusuma yānakiti hati,
hāḥ ṅ anaṅga mamanaḥ mamarimisi*

mwaŋ-ŋ-ikaŋ kayu kabèḥ paḍa mamanaḥ,
ronya yāpĕs alaris ya taji tajĕm,
pāŋ nya yéka larasa nya-ya malurus,
wruḥ nya yan tuju hatiṅku kĕna rujit*

mandamāruta miriṙ ya maṅiriri,
wāsita nya waṅi niŋ wana kusuma,
citta yāpuy umurub tĕhĕṙ apanas,
hāḥ lukan lara nikiŋ priyawiraha*

cāla ron ikana taŋ kayu tumayuŋ,
yoṅgwaniŋ bun aputiḥ makatiritis,
mutyahāra juga riŋ gaganatala,
n-ton ikā drawa hatiṅku juga tĕñuḥ*

hāḥ kapan kunaŋ iké kahuwusana,
mukti duḥka nikanaŋ priyawiraha,
kālamrĕtyu malalis tan anumata,
tan patīn aku huwus kasula-sula*

Śabda niŋ bhramara matta ya Apuya,
yak rĕṅö ya mahuyaŋ hati mapanas,
tulya paṙwwata sĕḍĕŋ matunu murub,
tan hanāta śaraṇāṅkwa manuluṅa*

mogha mohita hatiṅku ya wulaṅun,
n-ton alas ya manĕḍĕŋ masĕkaṙ arūm,
pomahan niraŋ anaṅga juga katon,
yak pramāda kasasaṙ ta kunĕŋ ari*

paŋ nikaŋ kayu tinūb niŋ aṅin alon,
naṙttakī ya maṅigĕl kayu mamijaḥ,
daṙppa taŋ bhramara matta maṅiduṅi,
wèt nyunĕṅku baribin-n-aku kabaran*

nā taṅis nira saŋ āṙyya raghusuta,
sandhi tībra maṅĕliḥ hati wipayoḥ,
rĕṣyamūka giri bhīṣaṇa masukĕt,
nā paran nira saśoka masusupan*

{basantatilaka}:6.130
