tatkāla yaṙ tĕka rikaŋ giri rĕṣyamūka,
sugrīwa śoka sira tībra maṅön akiṅkiŋ,
saŋ rāmabhadra śaraṇā wĕgilĕṅkwa tan len,
nā liŋ nirān laku manāsaka śīghra maṅkat*

tāmoli riŋ malaya paṙwwata duṙggamāwān,
yékā paran nira lawan bala wānarākwèḥ,
bhakti nya maprabhu dumĕḥ ya kabèḥ tumūta,
sugrīwa sādhu tuwi yogya siwin hiḍĕp nya*

sāmpun ḍatĕŋ dadi kinon ta siraŋ hanūmān,
dūtomarā ri sira saŋ raghuputra pètĕn,
tātaṙ wihaŋ pawanaputra kinon lumakwa,
yékan pĕsat nira rikaŋ gaganāntarāla*

riŋ rĕṣyamūka dunuṅĕn-n-ira śīghra mādrĕs,
humyus mĕsĕs Aṅin-aṅin-n-ira bāyubajra,
śīṙṇnékanaŋ kayu katūb mananā kabèḥ rūg,
sĕmpal papal kaparapal kapupuḥ pukaḥ puḥ*

n-ton téka saŋ raghusutāsusupan bhramanta,
maṅsö ta saŋ pawanaputra wawaŋ ta mojar*

hé sādhu dibya kita dhīra wĕnaŋ marā ṅké,
atyanta duṙggama nikiŋ giri rĕṣyamūka,
saŋ hyaŋ mahéśwara tuwin malĕmĕḥ marā ṅké,
ndyānuŋ prayojana Iké panusupta kāliḥ*

lwiṙ niŋ bhayātiśaya rodra Anuŋ hana ṅké,
muṅgwiŋ guhām hana ta rākṣasa lèn piśāca,
lāwan paran kari hawanta sukĕt-t-agamya,===
wwaŋ lén saké kita taman hana wèḥ mara ṅké*

kwèḥ siṅha sāhasa musuḥ niŋ asiŋ marā ṅké,
krūrāṅawit ya mawiṅit muruṅūtikaŋ moŋ,
maṅgā Umuṅgaḥ irikaŋ giri duṙggamāwān,
wuṅkal galintuŋ agaliŋ gumuliŋ iṅambaḥ*

malwā malok pĕluk ikaŋ lwaḥ aluṅka-luṅka,
molĕk ya kolĕk akèlĕm kumĕlem umĕntas,

dé niŋ mahāgaja lanā mara daṙppa madyus*

makwèḥ anuŋ bhaya nikaŋ giri bhīṣaṇa nké,
lāwan śilātala tĕla nya malā Ulā nya,
moŋ māṅsabhakṣa kaharĕp nya humöŋ galak nya,
tan wismayan paṅĕbusan mamisan wiṣa nya*

nā liŋ niraŋ pawanaputra mastö matakwan,
mojaṙ ta saŋ raghusutāṙ pawaraḥ rikaŋ don,
Ꜽ arya don mami nihan ta-rĕṅé tat aṅsö,
mwaŋ hétu niŋ malarasan ya ta pājarankwa*

kyātīŋ sarāt daśaratha prabhu saṙwwabhoga,
salwiṙ nikaŋ suka wiśéṣa hané sirākwèḥ,
akwèḥ anak nira Ariṅku ya dibyaśakti,
aṅhiŋ ṅhuluñ juga Anak nira mandabhāgya*

saṅké pakon ira marā riŋ alas malaṅghya,
yékā nimitta mami yan panusup ya kāliḥ,
luṅhā mĕgil kami riŋ āśrama saŋ sutikṣṇa,
ṅkā ta tamolaḥ aṅĕmit patapan prayatna*

sītā priyāṅku rasikā ta duluṙkkwi ṅūni,

sītā sirékana pinèt mami kām para ṅké,
ṇā hétu niŋ masusupan n Umahas bhramanta*

nojaṙ niraŋ raghusutāṙ pawaraḥ rikaŋ don,
mājaṙ-ajaṙ ta sumiliḥ ta siraŋ hanūmān,
Ꜽ rāghawa ṅhulun iké ta kinon marā ṅké,
sugrīwanāma kapirāja makon amèta*

prastāwa yéka huniṅan hana wānarāgöŋ,
śakti nya taṙ papaḍa śūra ṅaranya bālī,
Āditya soṙ ta sira dé nikanāŋ prabhāwa,
krodhāgalak ya paribhūta riké tuhanku*

miṅgat siromara rikaŋ malaya pradéśa,
maprītya don ira makon ta siromarā ṅké,
mahyun tamolaha sumiwya sukunta nātha*

mitrānta yogya sira liṅku Anugrahāna,
Āpan mahābala mahāṙddhika sādhubuddhi,
tūtūta māsiha mituhwa Asiŋ pakonta,
milwomatī daśamuka pramukā sirèŋ praŋ*

nāmhaŋ n ujaṙ nira ta saŋ anilātmajaswī,
tātaṙ wihaŋ daśarathātmaja śīghra maṅkat,
sāṅkat nirātiśaya haṙṣa ta saŋ hanūmān,
saŋ rāmadéwa hiniḍĕp nira kalpawrĕkṣa*

praptèŋ gunuŋ malaya saŋ nrĕpaputra rāma,
rĕŋrĕŋ paḍām nira panaḥ nira yéka mégha,
bālī diwākara samopaśamāmatī ya,
sugrīwa yéka mapanas ya maṅöb ikaŋ hrū*

tatkīmla yaṙ patĕmu kāliḥ amoŋ sirāpuy,

sāmpun nirāsamaya kapwa sahaṙṣa kāliḥ,
māṅĕn-naṅĕn ta sira kapwa mamèt upāya*

naŋ rāmadéwa mulat iŋ bala wānarākwèḥ,

polaḥ nya hūŋ nya gumuruḥ maturū rikaŋ pāŋ,
yékā dumèḥ nira sukā magiraŋ tumon ya*

sāmpun tĕguḥ rika pamitra nirāta kāliḥ,
mojaṙ ta saŋ prawara wānararāja mitra,
hé rāghawātiśaya śakti nikaŋ kapīndra,
bālī taman hana paḍa nya rikaŋ triloka*

tan saṅka riŋ paribhawéki wuwusku nātha,

byaktān pĕjaḥ nya tuwi dé ni panaḥta śakti*

nyānuŋ dumèḥ nika manĕmwa wiśéṣa riŋ rāt,

cittaṅku niśchaya Awās ya pati nya dènta*

bālī ya lāgi mamatī manikĕp gajéndra,

{Śikhariṇī}:6.160

saluṅha saŋ rāmāṙ laku mara ri kiṣkiṇḍha wiwara,
lawan saŋ sugrīwātirabhasa sahāsaŋ kinasigan,
katon taŋ lyaŋ malwām giriwara guhā ghora madalĕm,
kaḍatwan saŋ bālī pratibhaya lawaŋ nyādbhuta pĕtĕŋ*

siraŋ sugrīwāgyāsyaŋ i kaka niromĕtwa malagā,
humuŋ makrak krūra bhrukuṭi kuṭilāhyām sira ri hèŋ,
umaṅkat saŋ bālī mĕtu ta sira saṅkĕŋ giri guhām,
malĕs makrak pūṙṇnāŋ gaganatala digdéśa hibĕkan*

humuŋ humrĕŋ maṅsö ta sira kadi ta wyāghra magalak,
lawan saŋ sugrīwogratara kadi siṅhāṅrĕpa maṅaŋ,
masö madwandwāprĕp magarut asahut kapwa manikĕp,
manampyal maṅrĕṅgut paḍa ta sira gut-gūtĕn abutĕŋ*

rumukrūk taŋ rambut ginĕrĕmus umuṅgwiŋ palipisan,

humis mamwas taŋ rāḥ drawa ya mapisan syuk nya ri pipi,
tibā riŋ bāhwalwā ri ḍaḍa kaharan kumkuma mabāŋ*

makin daṙppān paprĕp ta maṅuwil iruŋ riŋ kuku makas,

hanan pamrĕp jaṅgut paḍa kapisahut huntwa maṅani,
anèkārūpékaŋ kira-kira ya kapwāṅutitakĕn*

saka kwĕḥ saŋ yogī matapa tĕpi niŋ paṙwwata kabèḥ,

mahas māmèt kĕmbaŋ mari ya sakarĕŋ kapwa ya milu,
siraŋ monāmomo mari muna manonton paḍa humuŋ*

pijeṙ saŋ rāmāṙ ton ta sira mataruŋ kapwa ta bĕtaḥ,

kalépyan saŋ rāmāṙ miṅĕt-iṅĕtakĕn maṅkin alupa,
wuruŋ tékaŋ tāṅan tumihaŋ apatan wruḥ riŋ uliha*

siraŋ sugrīwānliḥ tuwi kalalaḥ aṅkèṙ sira tĕkā,
awak rĕñcĕm tāmbis mati sira gĕlānāṙ pinipitan,
dudut tékā tĕṇḍas nira tuwi tinuṇḍĕs hinapitan,
umunduṙ méraŋ kapwa malara siroruk mamuruṅut*

mulat saŋ rāma r-ton ta sira tĕka rūkṣāṙddha mawĕnĕs,
masö śīghrānĕmbaḥ ta ri suku niraŋ rāmawijaya,
aḥ-o swāmī mithyāsamaya kita hāḥ madwa riŋ ujar,
ndya hétu nyāt tonton palaga mami tātan lĕkasi ya*

wawaŋ mojaṙ saŋ śrī raghusuta ri saŋ wānarapati,
nihan prastāwa nyān kadi ta nirapékṣāku humĕnĕŋ,
sèḍĕŋ tāprĕp tonton kita sadrĕśa rūpanta ya paḍa,

saŋ hyaŋ wé tuwi mapanas ta-ṅöb pwa ta ṅké,
yan sāmpun marĕn apanas lumakwa śīghra*

nyaŋ kumbaŋ ya rĕṅö-rèṅönta daṙppa moni,

tontonĕn-n Aku kalalaḥ pwa dènta ṅūni,
bhāgyaṅkun tĕka kita bāyuputra tan lèn*

nā liŋ niŋ gunuŋ asayut ri saŋ hanūmān,
wèt niŋ gyā nira sumahuṙ wawaŋ ta mojar,
hé ménāka giri huwus ta haywa képwan,
prĕgyākun samaya baṭa ara rāma magyā*

tāmolin kita ta samīraṇā ta mitra,
ndā magyām wruha ri si rāwaṇāku maṅké,
māpa pwékana muka niŋ ŋ inaṅluḥ iŋ rāt,
śakti nyékana papagākĕṅkwa yan prawrra*

sakwèḥ nyāŋ suraripu rākṣasolihaṅkwa,
ṣwasthā niŋ bhuwana sadhya déṅku tan lèn,   ❌
nī liŋ saŋ pawanasutomibĕṙ ta luṅhā*

{bramitākṣara}:8.18

hana rākṣasī katĕmu dé nira lén,

manikĕp-p Iwak ya pinaṅanya lanā*

kadi tuhwa śakti ya wĕnaŋ rabhasa*

raghuputra ṅūni mawuwus ri sira*

mamasaŋ-masaŋ-ŋ Aji sirĕp sisulap*

ininum nya rāḥ wija-wijaḥ mawĕrö,

{śālinī}:8.59

nāhan lwiṙ niŋ paṙhyaṅan ṅkī ri lĕṅkā,

atha sĕḍĕŋ umurub Ikū saŋ hanūmān umaṅkak tikāwak nirāgöŋ gunuŋ méru tulyānanāŋ nāgapāśāpasaḥ sāk pasātus tataś śiṙṇna rampuŋ pĕgat dénikā bāhu saŋ bāyuputromĕsat śīghra Ākāśagāmī miriṙ tāŋ aṅin ghora yāghūṙṇnitādrĕs riwutpāta humyus musus yomĕlĕk taŋ lĕbu,
kadi ta Inububan ya maṅkin murub tékanékū nirāpan katūb dé nikaŋ bāyubajré sĕḍĕŋ nyāṙ ibĕṙ tulya saŋ hyaŋ lĕmaḥ maṅlayaŋ mwaŋ apuy kyāti kālāgni rodrāṙ dunuŋ taŋ umaḥ ṅkā riŋ antaḥ purāpūṙwwa rūpa nya saśrī saśobhā yatékān tinunwan nirānéka waṙṇna nya nānāwidha*    ❌
paḍa makaparupuḥ ṅ-apuy yan dilaḥ riŋ umaḥ kapwa rĕmpak rĕmukmaṅkana ŋ maṇḍapāpan parĕŋ yan katunwan saka nyomakin wrĕddhitékaŋ apuy Ujwalālola kūmĕlab dīlaḥ nya lāṅit niṙbhāyātaḥ mānaḥ san hānūman mūlat kadbhūtékaŋ wātĕk rakṣāsé soṙ kāsoran kāśūran kāwīrankādhīran tuwi,    ❌
pa ḍa ta ya mututuŋ tutuk nyān kagöman kapūhan tumĕṅhāmtakut n-tonkaḍatwan katunwan kutug taŋ apuy loṙ kidul kālamrĕtyūpama nyomaladtan dilaḥ tulya télat nya molaḥ mĕlĕk taŋ kukus Aṙddha mawyaŋ-wyaṅèkĕl-jikèl yéka rambut ni tĕṇḍas nya rodrān katon kātara ŋ rākṣasā ghūṙṇni-tāwū humuŋ*
tripura-pura murub tinunwan bhaṭāréśwarānuŋ paḍa nyān tĕñuḥ tāṅumaḥ mās ya masyūḥ masāk taŋ sakāgöŋ maṇik bajra bajropama nyānmakas kāsyasiḥ tékanāŋ apsarī riŋ purāpūṙwwa yaṙ ton apuy kapwatékāgupuy kwèḥ kapĕyĕḥ gĕyuḥ yan kayuḥ kèn i cèṭi nya maṅluḥ umaṅguḥ huyaŋ yāṅliḥ,   ❌
talaga-talaga riŋ kaḍatwan winatwan ya dé niŋ maṇik candrakānté daṅū ndan mĕné śuṣka yāsāt ya kèsĕp sĕkaṙ niŋ aśokāṅasut yan kasūban panasrūkṣa sakwèḥ nya yākiŋ makiṅkiŋ manuk nyānaṅis moni kolāhalāwū walācakrawākā gĕlāna ŋ pĕluŋ haṅsa māśā saśokāswarāsū Ikaŋ sārasa*   ❌
